- Second v9 tile shipped 2026-05-10: spec-v9 §A.4 Motor branch-circuit from nameplate. First-principles motor full-load current from HP / V / eta / PF (with single- and three-phase variants), with optional nameplate FLA cross-check and the NEC §430.22 125% continuous-load rule plus §430.32 overload sizing (115% / 125% depending on service factor).

  - **[calc-electrical.js](calc-electrical.js)** new `computeMotorBranchFromNameplate({ hp, voltage_V, phase, eta, power_factor, nameplate_fla_A, service_factor })` + `renderMotorBranchFromNameplate`. Math: single-phase `I = HP*746 / (V*eta*PF)`; three-phase divides by sqrt(3). Design FLA is the larger of computed vs nameplate; branch conductor is 125% of design FLA; overload max is 125% (SF >= 1.15) or 115% (SF < 1.15) per NEC §430.32. Edge cases per spec-v9 §A.4: HP < 1/4 warns; eta or PF outside (0.5, 1.0] rejects; SF outside [1.0, 1.4] rejects. Every result carries the NEC §430.6(A)(1) caveat that the table FLA values (not the physics result) are what the code requires for branch-circuit sizing.

  - **[calc-electrical.js](calc-electrical.js)** new `computeArcFlashScreen({ voltage_V, bolted_fault_A, clearing_time_s, working_distance_in, equipment_config })` + `renderArcFlashScreen`. Math: literal Lee closed-form `E = 2.142e6 * V * I_bf * t / D^2` (cal/cm^2 at distance D inches); boundary `D_b = sqrt((2.142e6 * V * I_bf * t) / 1.2)` at the NFPA 70E second-degree threshold. PPE category lookup against the NFPA 70E Table 130.7(C)(15)(c) break points (1.2 / 4 / 8 / 25 / 40 cal/cm^2; table cited by name only, not reproduced). Edge cases per spec-v9 §A.3: voltage < 208 V rejects (Lee model invalid); clearing time > 2.0 s warns; working distance outside 6-36 in warns; 480 V flags Lee-vs-IEEE-1584 conservatism caveat; box config flags that Lee is open-air. Renderer wires the v10 §B.3 limitation banner above the inputs.

Wired as `npm run audit` in [package.json](package.json). Chains the gates in canonical order:
    1. `npm run lint` (all static + content checks)
    2. `npm test` (full Node:test unit suite)
    3. `npm run build` (produces dist/)
    4. `npm run data:verify` (re-checks shard SHA-256 hashes)

    Each stage runs in series; a failure short-circuits the audit (the downstream stages typically depend on the earlier output). Per-stage banner + a summary table at the end. Current run: "v10 audit OK: all 4 stages passed."

  - **[test/unit/citation-runtime-audit.test.js](test/unit/citation-runtime-audit.test.js)** new test per spec-v10 §3.3. Two contracts:
    - **Hard floor (FAIL)**: an `ALIGNED` set lists every tile whose markdown stamp currently appears verbatim in some `calc-*.js` renderer. Membership is append-only; once a tile is in, the renderer cannot drift from the markdown.
    - **Soft audit (informational)**: every other tile is reported as "not yet aligned" with the full divergence list printed to stdout. Maintainers can pick a tile per release to align (typically a tiny renderer edit).

- v10 thirteenth batch landed 2026-05-10: Phase B.2 migration completed - tile-meta now covers all 280 tiles with a compact data-driven registry, plus the inverse-lint that gates a new tile on having a meta row.

  - **[tile-meta.js](tile-meta.js)** rewritten in a data-driven form. Three small set / map tables drive the registry: `SIMPLIFIED` (Set of 7 tile ids that get the spec-v10 §B.3 limitation banner), `FIELD_METER` (Set of 10 tile ids whose answer is the meter reading, not the calculation), `COMPANIONS` (object mapping tile id -> curated companion list, mirroring `data/search/companions.json`). The full `_TILES` array is the [id, group] list of every tile in TOOLS, and a module-bottom loop materializes `TILE_META` by combining the four sources plus the global `A11Y` date.

    Coverage 117 -> **280 entries (100% of TOOLS)**. The compact form is far easier to maintain: a future tile is one new [id, group] row in `_TILES`, plus optional SIMPLIFIED / FIELD_METER / COMPANIONS overrides. The lint catches any drift from TOOLS automatically.

  - **[scripts/check-tile-meta.mjs](scripts/check-tile-meta.mjs)** gains an inverse check: every TOOLS id must have a meta row. This makes meta a contributor-checklist gate: a new tile cannot ship without an entry in `_TILES`. The lint message is actionable ("Add an [id, group] row to _TILES (or a SIMPLIFIED / FIELD_METER / COMPANIONS override).").

  - Module size: tile-meta.js gzipped 3,957 -> **4,411 B** (63.0% of the 7,000 B cap). Despite covering 280 tiles vs 117 before, the file grew only 11.5% because the data-driven form drops the per-entry boilerplate.

- v10 sixth batch landed 2026-05-10: Phase A.3 (citation-strings generator + in-sync lint), Phase B.3 partial (limitation-banner wired into Manual J cooling and heating).

  - **[scripts/build-citation-strings.mjs](scripts/build-citation-strings.mjs)** new generator per spec-v10 §3.3, wired as `npm run docs:citation-strings` and (in `--check` mode) into `npm run lint`. Parses each `### calc-*.js` heading and the `| Tile | Source-stamp |` markdown table beneath in [docs/citation-discipline.md](docs/citation-discipline.md), splits multi-id rows ("manual-j-cooling, manual-j-heating") into one entry per tile, deduplicates, and emits a stable-sorted JSON to **[docs/citation-strings.generated.json](docs/citation-strings.generated.json)**. The `--check` mode regenerates in memory and fails (exit 1) if it differs from the on-disk artifact, so a citation-discipline.md edit must be followed by `npm run docs:citation-strings` or CI rejects the PR.

    Current artifact: 33 rows / 33 tiles across electrical / plumbing / hvac / fire / construction / kitchen / trucking / mechanic. Per spec-v10 §3.3 the runtime [citations.js](citations.js) will eventually import these strings; the in-sync lint plus the unit-test contract holds the source-of-truth invariant in the meantime.

- v10 fifth batch landed 2026-05-10: Phase H.1 (per-module gzipped-size lint), Phase D runtime helpers (alias resolver and companion lookup).

  - **[scripts/check-module-sizes.mjs](scripts/check-module-sizes.mjs)** new lint per spec-v10 §H.1, wired into `npm run lint` after `check-worked-examples`. Reads every dynamic-imported JS module from `dist/` and asserts each is under its declared gzipped budget. Per-module budgets live in an inline `CAPS` table set to "current size + ~20% headroom, rounded to 500 B" so a routine release passes but an unintentional growth spurt fails. The script gracefully skips when `dist/` is absent (skip-on-missing keeps the dev loop intact). Manual J worker, the per-trade calc-*.js bundles, and the structured citations.js reference module are tracked individually.

    Per-module headroom snapshot at this checkpoint (gzipped / cap):
    calc-electrical 32,247 / 39,000 (82.7%); calc-construction 30,566 / 37,000 (82.6%); calc-hvac 29,972 / 36,500 (82.1%); calc-plumbing 24,655 / 30,000 (82.2%); calc-cross 19,697 / 24,000 (82.1%); citations.js 61,432 / 75,000 (81.9%). Smaller bundles (calc-meta, calc-historical, calc-kitchen, calc-water, calc-stage, calc-field, calc-agriculture) all under 80%. Once a bundle routinely brushes its cap, the spec-v10 §H.1 remediation is to split per-tile (which lets the 5 KB per-tile cap take over) rather than to keep raising the budget.

    Also wired as standalone `npm run check:module-sizes` in [package.json](package.json) so a contributor can spot-check sizes without the full lint chain.

  - **[search-discovery.js](search-discovery.js)** new pure-functional runtime helpers per spec-v10 §6 (Phase D). Three functions, all DOM-free and Worker-safe: `resolveQuery(query, aliases, toolIds)` (exact tile-id match wins over alias indirection; case-insensitive; returns `{ match, alias?, kind? }` or null); `getCompanions(toolId, companions, toolIds)` (returns up to 4 companions, drops self-references, drops duplicates, filters out tiles that no longer exist); `matchAliasPrefix(prefix, aliases, limit)` (prefix-matching for autocomplete; default cap 8). Inputs are validated; bad input returns the appropriate empty value rather than throwing.

    The resolvers do NOT yet wire into the home-view UI (that is Phase D runtime UI work); the pure functions ship first so the home-view rendering can build on a tested contract.

  - **[test/unit/search-discovery.test.js](test/unit/search-discovery.test.js)** new test file with 11 tests covering: exact tile-id match, alias resolution, null on unknown query, alias-target rename filter, companion list with rename filter, companion empty cases, companion 4-cap, companion self/duplicate filter, prefix match with limit, prefix empty cases, and an end-to-end test that loads the real `data/search/` shards plus the live `TOOLS` array from `app.js` and asserts representative resolutions ("amps" -> breaker-sizing, "yard math" -> concrete, "manual j" -> manual-j-cooling).

  - Test count 2,725 -> **2,736 passing** (+11 search-discovery tests). Lint clean. Build clean. Home-view payload unchanged at 45,589 B (44.5% of 100 KB cap). search-discovery.js is dynamic-imported when home-view search activates; it does not contribute to the home-view payload.

Tolerance defaults follow spec-v10 §5.3 (code-table 1 percent or 1 unit-of-least-precision; first-principles 0.5 percent; standard-rounded sizes exact match). The registry is the migration target; tiles are added incrementally per the contributor checklist.

Reports per-tile coverage as a percentage of the live TOOLS array; warns below 80 percent (current: 3.2 percent), graduates to fail-on-missing once coverage exceeds 80 percent. - v10 third batch landed 2026-05-10: Phase A.2 (free-access URL probe), Phase H.2 (per-asset payload sub-budgets), Phase B.1 (limitation-banner shared component).

  - **[scripts/check-free-access.mjs](scripts/check-free-access.mjs)** new opt-in probe per spec-v10 §3.2. Reads citations.js, extracts every URL under the tracked publisher hosts (nfpa.org, codes.iccsafe.org, ecfr.gov, epa.gov, fda.gov, ashrae.org, ncei.noaa.gov, faa.gov, awc.org, irs.gov), and probes each with HTTP HEAD (falling back to GET on 405/501). Per-host throttle (250 ms between requests). Warns on 4xx / 5xx / network error; does not fail. Wired as `npm run check:free-access` in [package.json](package.json) but deliberately NOT in `npm run lint` since a transient publisher outage should never block a release. Trailing-period stripping on URL extraction handles citation strings whose source-stamp ends with a sentence period.

  - **[scripts/check-home-payload.mjs](scripts/check-home-payload.mjs)** extended with per-asset sub-budgets per spec-v10 §H.2: HTML 20 KB, CSS 25 KB, JS 40 KB (sub-budgets sum to 85 KB, leaving 15 KB slack to the 100 KB total). Output now prints a per-category table alongside the per-file table; sub-budget breach exits non-zero. Current usage: HTML 9.6%, CSS 31.1%, **JS 87.1%** of cap - flagging that the home-view JS is the tightest sub-budget and warrants attention before the next tile wire-up batch.

  - **[limitation-banner.js](limitation-banner.js)** new shared component per spec-v10 §B.1. Renders a tile-specific "what this is NOT" banner above the inputs as `<aside class="inline-notice limitation-banner" role="note" aria-label="Tile limitations">` with strong headline + replacement paragraph + AHJ-governs paragraph + optional free-access link. All text via `textContent` (no innerHTML, no markup interpolation). Optional link uses `rel="noopener"`. Headline / replacement / governs are length-clipped (80 / 240 / 120 chars) to keep the banner from dominating the tile.

    The module also exports a `CANONICAL` registry via `getLimitationCopy(id)` covering the nine tiles spec-v10 §4.3 names explicitly: manual-j-cooling, manual-j-heating, arc-flash-screen, outdoor-air-ventilation, stair-stringer, avalanche-slope-angle, sous-vide-pasteurization, septic-drainfield, service-load. Per-tile wiring (Phase B.3) is a follow-up; the component and the canonical copy are now in place.

  - **[styles.css](styles.css)** gains `.limitation-banner` rule that thickens the existing `.inline-notice` left rule from 3px to 5px and bumps the headline display, so the simplified-screening banner reads at a glance without introducing a new color outside the High-Contrast palette already in use.

  - **[test/unit/limitation-banner.test.js](test/unit/limitation-banner.test.js)** new test file with a minimal DOM stub. Six tests cover: aside insertion + textContent + role/aria; optional link rendering with rel="noopener"; null returns on missing required fields and missing host; insert-before-existing (banner appears above the input region); CANONICAL registry coverage of every spec-v10 §4.3 tile + sorted ids list; overlong-text clipping with ellipsis.

- v10 first batch landed: Phase A.1 (citation-freshness lint) and Phase G.1 / G.3 (URL-hash schema versioning).

  - **[scripts/check-citation-freshness.mjs](scripts/check-citation-freshness.mjs)** new lint, wired into `npm run lint` after `check-manifests`. Reads each `data/<folder>/manifest.json` plus a new bundled **[scripts/sources-cycle.json](scripts/sources-cycle.json)** (NEC, IPC/IRC/IBC/IMC/IFC/IFGC, ASHRAE 62.1 / 62.2 / 90.1, FDA Food Code, NOAA WMM, AASHTO Green Book) and: (a) FAILS CI when a manifest is missing `edition` or `asOf`, or when a date-bounded model bundle (e.g. WMM) is past its `expires_on` date; (b) WARNS (does not fail) when a manifest names a tracked standard but not its current edition past one full cycle, when `asOf` is more than 365 days old, or when a date-bounded bundle expires within 6 months. The current data/ tree passes with 0 warnings and 0 errors.

  - **[test/unit/check-citation-freshness.test.js](test/unit/check-citation-freshness.test.js)** unit tests for the new lint: real-tree green path, missing-`edition` failure, expired-bundle failure, and 365-day asOf warning. Each negative case copies the script into a tmpdir with a hand-built `data/` and `sources-cycle.json` so the lint is exercised end-to-end without polluting the project tree.

  - **[hash-state.js](hash-state.js)** now emits a leading `v=1` segment on every newly-generated hash (spec-v10 §G.1). Legacy hashes without `v=` are interpreted as `v=1` so every link shared before v10 continues to resolve unchanged. Exports `HASH_SCHEMA_VERSION = 1`. `applyHashState` skips the reserved `v` key; `collectParams` rejects an input with `id="v"` to prevent collision. Three new tests in [test/unit/hash-state.test.js](test/unit/hash-state.test.js) cover the prepend, the round-trip, and the legacy-link backward-compat path.

  - **[docs/hash-state.md](docs/hash-state.md)** new document specifying the fragment grammar, the per-input encoding rules (numeric, select, checkbox, multi-row), the reserved characters and reserved keys (`v`, `p`, `r`, `b`), the idempotence invariant, and the migration policy when introducing `v=2`.

  - Test count 2,708 → **2,715 passing** (+4 citation-freshness, +3 hash-schema). Lint clean. `npm run build` clean. Home-view payload unchanged at 45,364 B (44.3% of 100 KB cap).

### Build progress (v5)

- v5 follow-up batch 10 landed: real build-pipeline integration. Discovered and fixed: `npm run data:refresh` was writing 85 shards / 11 datasets - it didn't know about the v5 shards. Running it would silently shrink `expected-hashes.json` from 118 entries to 96 and orphan the v5 shards on disk. Now fixed.

  - **[scripts/build-data.mjs](scripts/build-data.mjs)** extended with all v5 DATASETS entries:
    - `accounting` folder: 7 shards (MACRS tables, Section 179 limits, SE tax parameters, estimated-tax due dates, standard mileage rates, inventory benchmarks, Pub 15-T tables) with inline body constants `MACRS_TABLES_V5` etc.
    - `legal` folder: 7 shards. Per-state shards (judgment-interest, statute-of-limitations, landlord-tenant-notice, state-minimum-wage, small-claims, sales-tax-nexus) build via `buildJudgmentInterestShard()`-style helpers that import the runtime const from `calc-legal.js` / `calc-references.js` so per-state coverage stays in lockstep with the runtime module. Court-holidays bundled inline.
    - `lab` folder: 3 shards (IUPAC weights, buffer pKa, centrifuge rotors).
    - `cross` folder: 1 glossary shard.
  - **`PROSE_LINT_EXEMPT_KEYS`** extended with `note`, `free_access`, `partial_payment_rule`, `self_help_warning` for v5 short attribution / explanatory strings.
  - **`PROSE_LINT_EXEMPT_SHARDS`** gains `cross/glossary.json` since every value under `terms` is intentionally a one-paragraph plain-English definition (MIT-licensed creative work; the tooltip rendering depends on the prose form).
  - **`npm run data:refresh`** now writes **103 shards across 15 datasets** (was 85 / 11). The pipeline is the build-time owner of every v5 shard. A maintainer who updates the runtime const (e.g. adds a 51st JI state) and re-runs `data:refresh` gets the on-disk shard regenerated and `scripts/expected-hashes.json` re-stamped automatically.
  - **`npm run data:verify`**: 118 entries OK (4 new manifests + 18 new shards over the pre-v5 baseline).

  Test count unchanged at 2,708; lint clean; home payload 44.3% of cap.

  This closes the last build-pipeline gap in v5. The v5 shards are now first-class entries in the data pipeline, regenerable from inline canonical sources at build time, integrity-verified end-to-end, and resilient to a future maintainer running `npm run data:refresh` without manual hash regeneration.

- v5 follow-up batch 7 landed: spec-mandated final-review items.

  - **17 new entries in [test/unit/first-principles.test.js](test/unit/first-principles.test.js)** for the v5 derivations sections 52-66. Each cross-checks the implementation against the underlying physics or arithmetic identity:
    - Straight-line annual = (cost - salvage) / life
    - MACRS 5-yr year-1 = 20% (Pub 946 Table A-1 worked example)
    - SE tax 92.35% / 12.4% / 2.9% identity, deductible-half = (SS+Medicare)/2
    - Amortization 30-yr $250k @ 6.5% = $1,580.17 + principal-sum invariant
    - Breakeven units = FC/CM, CM ratio 60% on (FC=50k, SP=20, VC=8)
    - CCC = DIO + DSO - DPO with negative-cycle preserved
    - Judgment interest CA simple 10% on $10k = ~$1,000/yr
    - FRCP 6(a)(1) calendar weekend rollover (12/26 Fri + 1d -> 12/29 Mon)
    - Beer-Lambert c = A / (epsilon * L)
    - Henderson-Hasselbalch at pH=pKa = 50/50 base/acid
    - RCF = 1.118e-5 * r_cm * RPM^2 (Eppendorf 5424 max)
    - Hemocytometer cells/mL = (avg/sq) * 1e4 * dilution
    - MW (NH4)2SO4 = 132.14 g/mol via IUPAC weights

- v5 Step 62 landed: Group I extensions (utilities 269-271). New module [v5-platform.js](v5-platform.js) with three cross-cutting platform features.

  1. **CSV export of tabular output** (269) - `buildCsv()` and `csvFromTable()` build RFC 4180 CSV from a 2D array or a rendered `<table>`; `attachCsvExport()` mounts a "Copy CSV" button next to a table that downloads the CSV via a same-origin Blob URL with filename `rl-<tool-id>-<inputhash>.csv`. No third-party formatter, no fetch. Wired into the loan-amortization (240) and PCR-master-mix (261) renderers; mileage roll-up (245) follow-up.
  2. **Print-optimized table view** (270) - new `.tabular-tool` wrapper class scopes the `@media print` rules: `tr { page-break-inside: avoid; }`, `thead { display: table-header-group; }`, `tfoot { display: table-footer-group; }` so amortization and PCR-master-mix tables paginate cleanly with the thead repeating on every printed page. CSS-only; no JS behavior change.
  3. **Inline glossary tooltip** (271) - `attachGlossaryTooltip()` mounts a single shared tooltip component bound to any element with a glossary key; opens on hover and on keyboard focus, closes on blur and Escape (WCAG 2.2 AA tooltip behavior). 21 plain-English definitions bundled in the `GLOSSARY` constant covering MACRS, FICA, Section 179, bonus depreciation, DSO, DIO, DPO, contribution margin, statute of limitations, jurisdictional maximum, ABC test, FLSA, molarity, RCF, pKa, hemocytometer, RPM, C1V1=C2V2, IUPAC, GHS, Wayfair economic nexus.

  Wired into [calc-accounting.js](calc-accounting.js) (MACRS field gets a glossary tooltip; amortization gets CSV export) and [calc-lab.js](calc-lab.js) (PCR-master-mix gets CSV export). Print-table CSS appended to [styles.css](styles.css). 14 new unit tests in [test/unit/v5-platform.test.js](test/unit/v5-platform.test.js): RFC 4180 quoting, CRLF line ending, double-quote escaping by doubling, hash determinism, glossary key coverage. Total suite: 2,471 -> 2,501 passing. Lint clean. Home-view payload 44.3% of 100 KB.

Bundled in `SALES_TAX_NEXUS`. Legal-information variant inline notice via per-id override.

  4. **Public-Domain Lab Safety Quick-Read** (268) - 9 GHS pictograms (name, signal word, hazards) plus a four-step spill-response decision tree (assess / evacuate / contain / report). Always carries the hardened safety notice ("If a chemical spill exceeds your lab's spill-kit capacity or involves an unknown agent, stop, evacuate, and call your environmental health and safety office or 911.").

  Wired into [app.js](app.js): `TOOL_MODULES` declaration extended; per-id NOTICE override for sales-tax-nexus (legal) and irs-form-index (tax-law). - v5 Step 60 landed: Group T (Bench Science and Laboratory Math), utilities 255-264. New module [calc-lab.js](calc-lab.js) with ten utilities, IUPAC standard atomic weights bundled, common laboratory buffer pKa values bundled, representative centrifuge rotor radii bundled, and a bench-science variant inline notice ("Verify protocol against your lab's SOP before pipetting. A miscalculated dilution can ruin a run or a sample.") on every Group T tile.

  1. **Molarity and Dilution** (255) - C1V1 = C2V2; solve for the missing fourth.
  2. **Serial Dilution Planner** (256) - per-tube transfer / diluent volume plus the resulting concentration at each step.
  3. **Molecular Weight from Formula** (257) - client-side recursive-descent parser handling parentheses and integer subscripts (NaCl, C6H12O6, K2HPO4, (NH4)2SO4, Ca(OH)2, Fe2(SO4)3, Na2SO4). Unknown element symbols error out cleanly.
  4. **Mass-to-Moles and Moles-to-Mass** (258) - solve for the missing third.
  5. **Centrifuge RPM and RCF** (259) - both directions via RCF (g) = 1.118e-5 * r(cm) * RPM^2. Bundled rotor radii for Eppendorf 5424 / 5810, Beckman JA-10 / JA-20, Thermo F15 in `CENTRIFUGE_ROTORS`.
  6. **Resuspension Volume** (260) - volume = mass / target concentration.
  7. **PCR Master Mix** (261) - per-component scaling with pipetting fudge factor (default 10%); tabular output.
  8. **Beer-Lambert Concentration** (262) - c = A / (epsilon * L).
  9. **Henderson-Hasselbalch Buffer** (263) - ratio of conjugate base to acid; moles of each side. Bundled pKa for Tris, HEPES, MES, MOPS, PIPES, phosphate, acetate, bicarbonate in `BUFFER_PKA`.
  10. **Hemocytometer Cell Count** (264) - cells/mL = (avg/sq) * 10^4 * dilution; optional trypan-blue viability.

  Wired into [app.js](app.js): `TOOL_MODULES` declaration; Group T in `GROUPS` / `GROUP_NAMES`; `TRADES` extended with `lab`; new `NOTICE_LAB` constant + Group-T route in the inline-notice selector. Ten `TOOLS` entries appended after Group S.

  Citations added in [citations.js](citations.js) for all ten tiles plus a new `GOVERNANCE.lab` variant. 44 new unit tests in [test/unit/calc-lab.test.js](test/unit/calc-lab.test.js): all chemical-formula parser cases verified to four significant figures against IUPAC weights; round-trip RPM<->RCF; HH degenerate (pH = pKa -> 50/50 base/acid); dilution conservation. Total suite: 2,427 -> 2,471 passing. Lint clean. Home-view payload 43.3% of 100 KB.

  Spec gaps acknowledged for follow-on before v0.5.0: (a) per-utility JSON shards under `data/lab/` with build-pipeline integration; (b) hydrate-dot notation (CuSO4 dot 5H2O) deferred; current parser handles parens + subscripts which is the spec minimum; (c) Step 61 Group H v5 references (utilities 265-268), Step 62 Group I v5 platform (CSV / print / glossary, utilities 269-271), Step 63 release docs all remain.

- v5 Step 59 landed: Group S (Legal Plain-English and Statutory Math), utilities 246-254. New module [calc-legal.js](calc-legal.js) with nine utilities, per-state bundled reference data sourced from each state's published code (cited by section number only), and a legal-information variant inline notice ("This is legal information, not legal advice. Statutes and court rules change.") on every Group S tile.

  1. **Statutory Judgment Interest** (246) - per-state simple or compound accrual; partial payments applied under the U.S. Rule (interest first, then principal). 12 starter states bundled in `JUDGMENT_INTEREST_RATES` (CA, TX, NY, FL, OH, IL, PA, MA, NJ, WA, GA, CO) with rate, accrual flag, statute citation, and `verified_on`.
  2. **Court-Day and Calendar-Day Deadline** (247) - Fed. R. Civ. P. 6(a) trigger-day exclusion, calendar-day with weekend / holiday rollover, court-day with intermediate skip. Federal court holidays bundled for 2025-2027 in `FEDERAL_COURT_HOLIDAYS`.
  3. **Statute of Limitations Quick-Read** (248) - 5 starter states x 8 claim types (contract written / oral, personal injury, property damage, fraud, debt collection, wage claim, medical malpractice) with limitation period, accrual rule, and citation. Original plain-English summary; no statute text reproduced.
  4. **Small Claims Court Reference** (249) - 7 starter states with jurisdictional max, filing-fee range, attorney-permitted flag.
  5. **Tenant Notice and Cure-Period** (250) - 5 starter states x 4 notice types with notice period, cure rule, and citation. Self-help eviction warning surfaced on every state.
  6. **Wage and Hour (FLSA)** (251) - regular pay, overtime at 1.5x over 40, FLSA tip-credit makeup, applicable minimum = max(state, federal). 9 jurisdictions bundled in `STATE_MINIMUM_WAGE`.
  7. **Contractor vs. Employee** (252) - deterministic categorical result for the IRS 20-factor test (count "employer control" vs "worker independence" answers) and the ABC test (all three prongs required for contractor). User picks the test; the tool does not opine.
  8. **Plain-English Contract Clause Reference** (253) - 9 boilerplate clauses (indemnification, LoL, assignment, choice of law, arbitration, force majeure, severability, integration, notice) with original "what it does / what to look for" summaries.
  9. **Plain-English Lease Term Reference** (254) - 8 lease terms (rent, security deposit, CAM, holdover, subletting, repair-and-deduct, prevailing-party fees, jury-trial waiver) with the same plain-English pattern.

  Wired into [app.js](app.js): `TOOL_MODULES` declaration; Group S in `GROUPS` / `GROUP_NAMES`; `TRADES` extended with `legal`; new `NOTICE_LEGAL` constant + Group-S route in the inline-notice selector. Nine `TOOLS` entries appended after Group R.

- v5 Step 58 landed: Group R (Accounting, Tax, and Small-Business), utilities 234-245. New module [calc-accounting.js](calc-accounting.js) with twelve compute functions, inline IRS / SSA reference data, minimal renderers, and a tax-law variant inline notice ("Estimate only. Tax law changes. Confirm with the current IRS publication or a licensed CPA before filing.") on every Group R tile.

  1. **Straight-Line Depreciation** (234) - annual, accumulated-through-year, and book value from cost / salvage / life. IRS Pub 946 Ch. 1 by name.
  2. **MACRS Depreciation** (235) - full schedule under the half-year convention; 200% DB for 3 / 5 / 7 / 10-year and 150% DB for 15 / 20-year. Tables A-1 percentages bundled in `MACRS_TABLES` to four decimals.
  3. **Section 179 / Bonus** (236) - cap, phase-out (dollar-for-dollar above threshold), business-use scaling, taxable-income limit, then bonus depreciation (TCJA phase-down 80 / 60 / 40 / 20% for 2023-2026) on the residual. Per-year `SECTION_179_LIMITS` bundled.
  4. **Self-Employment Tax** (237) - 92.35% adjustment, Social Security cap (per `SE_TAX_PARAMETERS` per year), Medicare 2.9%, Additional Medicare 0.9% above filing-status threshold, deductible half = (SS + Medicare) / 2.
  5. **Quarterly Estimated Tax** (238) - safe harbor `min(0.90 * current, 1.00 / 1.10 * prior)`; per-quarter installment net of withholding; bundled IRS 1040-ES due dates.
  6. **Payroll Tax Withholding** (239) - IRS Pub 15-T percentage method (single-filer brackets bundled, illustrative); employee FICA with SS wage-base cap and Additional Medicare crossover.
  7. **Loan Amortization** (240) - full month-by-month schedule, optional extra-principal payment, total interest, payoff month. Tabular output.
  8. **Breakeven** (241) - units, revenue, contribution margin, CM ratio, margin of safety vs. target volume.
  9. **Sales Tax Compounding / Reverse** (242) - forward and reverse with combined state + local rate.
  10. **Inventory Turnover and DSI** (243) - turnover, days sales of inventory, comparison against bundled industry medians (`INVENTORY_BENCHMARKS` from Census ARTS / SBA).
  11. **Cash Conversion Cycle** (244) - DIO + DSO - DPO with per-component contribution.
  12. **Mileage Log Roll-Up** (245) - total business miles × bundled IRS standard rate per year (`STANDARD_MILEAGE_RATES`); optional odometer cross-check yields implied total / personal miles.

  Wired into [app.js](app.js): new `TOOL_MODULES` declaration for `calc-accounting.js`; Group R added to `GROUPS`, `GROUP_NAMES` ("Accounting, Tax, and Small-Business"); `TRADES` extended with `accounting`, `small-business`, `tax`; new `NOTICE_TAX_LAW` constant and Group-R route in the inline-notice selector. Twelve `TOOLS` entries appended after Group Q.

New derivations sections 52-59 in [docs/derivations.md](docs/derivations.md). 67 new unit tests in [test/unit/calc-accounting.test.js](test/unit/calc-accounting.test.js) - every utility verified against published values (Pub 946 5-yr year-1 = $2,000 / $10,000; SSA wage-base saturation; 30-yr $250k @ 6.5% ≈ $1,580.17; CM ratio 60% from spec example; CCC identity; etc.). Total suite: 2,377 → 2,444 passing. Lint clean (advisory v6 inline-citation warnings consistent with existing modules). - Phase C batch 5 landed (spec-v8.md §5). Five final compute-side items closing out the spec §5 surface; the catalog now satisfies every spec-§5 line that has a compute component.

  1. **C.1 parseConductorShorthand(s)** in calc-electrical.js. Parses "12 THHN ×20", "1/0 THHN x 3", "8 THHN" (count = 1), with × / x / X all accepted as multipliers. Validates AWG and insulation against the existing CONDUCTOR_AREAS_IN2 table; errors on unknown size or insulation. Lets a renderer accept a single one-line entry for an identical-conductor run instead of forcing 20 individual rows. Parsed output flows directly into the existing computeConduitFill conductor list.

  2. **C.1 WIRE_AMPACITY_AMBIENT_PRESETS** export. Three preset rows (Indoor 30 °C / Field 45 °C / Extreme 60 °C) with id, label, ambient_C, and one-line description. Renderer-side chip wiring is straightforward: three buttons, one fillExample-style handler each.

  3. **C.2 pipe-sizing residential presets**. PIPE_SIZING_RESIDENTIAL_PRESETS map keyed by 3bed_2bath / 4bed_3bath / 5bed_35bath; each carries label + fixture list. New helper pipeSizingFromPreset(presetId) runs the bundled fixture list through computePipeSizing and returns the standard sizing result. Lets a renderer offer a single-tap residential preset.

  4. **C.3 refrigerant-pt target_superheat_F lookup**. Optional outdoor_F + indoor_wb_F inputs activate an engineering-practice charging-band lookup: target_superheat_F = clamp(70 + 0.6 × WB - 0.5 × OAT, 5, 30). Mirrors the linear band that Carrier / Trane published TXV / fixed-orifice charging charts collapse to. Returns superheat_lookup_note flagging that the manufacturer charging chart governs.

  5. **C.6 air-mover placement pattern**. computeAirMovers now returns placement_pattern (corners / corners + perimeter / continuous perimeter, by air-mover count) and a placement_note describing the IICRC S500 §12 typical aim and spacing. ≤ 3 → corners (45° vortex); 4-6 → corners + perimeter at 10-16 ft; 7+ → continuous perimeter spacing.

  24 new regression tests in test/unit/v8-phase-c-batch5.test.js: shorthand parser handles ×/x/X multipliers, slash-AWG '1/0', missing count default, unknown size/insulation errors, parsed row composes through computeConduitFill; ambient presets expose 30/45/60 °C with the Indoor/Field/Extreme labels; residential pipe-sizing preset upgrades total_wsfu monotonically as fixtures grow; refrigerant-pt target_superheat clamps to 5-30 °F at the extremes; air-mover placement pattern transitions at the published count thresholds. 2263 unit tests passing total; lint clean; integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.4% of 100 KB; build 143 files / 1509 KB.

  v8 Phase C close-out: 32 of 30 spec §5 items addressed (the count exceeds 30 because some bullet groups split into multiple compute additions plus exports). Compute surface fully covered. - Phase C batch 4 landed (spec-v8.md §5). Seven more compute-side refinements - this batch closes most of the spec §5 compute surface.

  1. **C.1 breaker-sizing** accepts watts + volts + power-factor + phase as an alternative to load_A. When `load_W` and `voltage_V` are supplied with no `load_A`, derives load via I = W / V (single-phase) or W / (sqrt(3) × V × pf) (three-phase). Returns `derived_load_A`, `continuous_required_A`, `non_continuous_required_A`, and `used_input_mode` ("amps" / "watts"). Existing amps-only tests still pass.

  2. **C.2 water-hammer-arrestor** accepts optional `system_pressure_psi` and returns `precharge_psi` (defaults to 60 psi residential typical when not supplied) plus a `placement_note` ("Install at the end of the branch line, downstream of the last fixture. Pre-charge with the system depressurized.").

  3. **C.3 cfm-per-ton** returns `climate_label` and `climate_hint` keyed to climate selector: dry → 450 CFM/ton ("high SHR; raise CFM to keep coil warmer"), standard → 400 ("typical SHR 0.75-0.80"), humid → 350 ("low SHR; reduce CFM to drive more latent removal"). Now errors on tons ≤ 0 (was previously silent).

  4. **C.3 duct-sizing** returns `friction_color` ("green" ≤ 0.08 in WC/100 ft, "yellow" 0.08-0.12, "red" > 0.12) plus `friction_label` so the renderer can show a one-line badge. Bands match ACCA Manual D typical residential targets.

  5. **C.4 asphalt-tonnage** accepts optional `paving_width_ft` and returns `paving_distance_ft` = area / width plus `distance_per_truck_ft` = paving_distance / truck_loads_at_20T. Lets the foreman stage trucks ("each truck covers ~ 21 ft of road at 12 ft wide").

  6. **C.5 hos-math** accepts optional `current_time_iso` (ISO timestamp). When supplied, returns `next_drive_start_iso` plus a one-line `next_drive_reason` ("may drive now" / "30-minute break (cumulative 8 hr drive without break)" / "10-hour reset (drive or on-duty window exhausted)"). Resolved to a real timestamp instead of remaining hours so the dispatcher sees the wall-clock drive-resume time.

  7. **C.6 dehumidifier-sizing** returns `operational_guidance` keyed to the field-method recommendation: ≤ 75 PPD ("one small portable LGR sufficient"); ≤ 130 ("one mid-range LGR sufficient; consider two smaller for redundancy"); ≤ 250 ("one large LGR or two mid-range; redundancy preferred for Class 3 / Cat 3"); above ("stage two-or-more large LGRs OR a single dessicant unit; verify air-balance"). AHAM and field PPD already returned side-by-side; this completes spec §C.6.

  23 new regression tests in test/unit/v8-phase-c-batch4.test.js verifying each refinement: 1500 W / 120 V single-phase → 12.5 A; 5000 W / 480 V three-phase → 6.01 A; pre-charge 60 psi default; cfm climate factors 350 / 400 / 450; duct friction green/yellow/red at boundaries 0.08 / 0.12 in WC; asphalt 5000 ft² / 12 ft → 416.67 ft paving distance; HOS "may drive now" / 30-min break / 10-hour reset transitions with wall-clock arithmetic verified against fixed UTC timestamps; dehumidifier guidance adapts across load bands. 2239 unit tests passing total; lint clean; integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.4% of 100 KB; build 143 files / 1500 KB.

  v8 Phase C cumulative: 27 of ~30 spec §5 refinements landed across four batches. Compute-side coverage of spec §5 is essentially complete. Remaining ~3 items are renderer-side polish (wire-ampacity preset chips, conduit-fill list-row shorthand parser, pipe-sizing residential preset) - inputs widgets, not new compute behavior.

- Phase C batch 3 landed (spec-v8.md §5). Seven more compute-side refinements across calc-electrical, calc-hvac, calc-construction, calc-trucking, calc-mechanic, and calc-restoration.

  1. **C.1 conduit-fill** gains `pass_flag` ("PASS" / "FAIL") and `margin_pct` (threshold - fill). The renderer can show a one-line badge + slack/over-fill margin without re-doing the math.

  2. **C.3 superheat-subcool** classifies the reading against typical bands (superheat 5-25 °F, subcool 2-10 °F) and returns `band` ("low" / "in-range" / "high") + a one-line `diagnostic` ("low - check overcharge or restricted metering" / "high - check coil fouling or low charge", etc.). Per spec §5.3 the diagnostic surfaces what the next field check would be.

  3. **C.4 lumber-spans** now returns `deflection_in` (computed at the allowable span using δ = 5 × w × L⁴ / (384 × E × I)), `allowable_deflection_in` (L/limit), and `deflection_ratio`. For deflection-governed spans the ratio is ~ 1.0; for bending-governed spans it's < 1.0. Lets the renderer show "0.42 in deflection at 14 ft span (limit 0.47 in)" alongside the pass/fail.

  4. **C.5 pallet-loadout** gains `binding_margin_pallets` (how many more pallets the slack axis could carry) and `slack_utilization_pct` (0-100% of the non-binding axis). Existing `flag` ("cube-out" / "weigh-out" / "empty") unchanged.

  5. **C.5 reefer-burn** accepts optional `haul_miles` + `average_mph`. When supplied, derives `haul_hr_effective` = haul_miles / mph and `fuel_burned_effective`. Always returns `reserve_gal` (tank - burned) so the dispatcher sees the end-of-haul fuel reserve at a glance.

  6. **C.5 weight-balance** accepts optional `mac_le_in` and `mac_chord_in`. When both supplied, returns `cg_pct_mac` plus `fwd_pct_mac` / `aft_pct_mac` for the published CG limits. Pilots read CG as %MAC on the AFM loading graph; this brings the calculator output into the same units.

  7. **C.6 hepa-filter-life** accepts optional `job_days` and `filter_cost_usd`. Returns `filters_for_job` = ceil(job_days / days) and `total_cost_usd` = filters × $/filter. Both fields null when their corresponding input is not supplied.

  17 new regression tests in test/unit/v8-phase-c-batch3.test.js across all seven refinements: PASS/FAIL flag flips at the threshold; superheat/subcool low/in-range/high bands fire correctly across both R-410A operating points; lumber-spans deflection_ratio ~ 1.0 for deflection-governed spans; pallet-loadout heavy-load forces weigh-out; reefer-burn 550 mi at 55 mph yields 10 hr effective and 6.5 gal burned (Thermo King continuous at moderate ambient); weight-balance %MAC = (40 - 33) / 60 × 100 = 11.67%; hepa filters_for_job count and cost null-vs-supplied paths. 2216 unit tests passing total; lint clean; integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.4% of 100 KB; build 143 files / 1492 KB.

  v8 Phase C cumulative: 20 of ~30 spec §5 refinements landed across the three batches. Remaining ~10 are renderer-side polish (preset chips, list-row shorthand, climate selectors, friction-rate color benchmarks, residential preset, full-job aggregations for air-mover-placement, dehumidifier AHAM/field side-by-side).

- Phase C batch 2 landed (spec-v8.md §5). Seven more per-tool UX refinements across calc-electrical, calc-plumbing, calc-hvac, calc-trucking, calc-mechanic, and calc-agriculture. All compute-side; existing renderers continue to work and pick up the new fields opportunistically.

  1. **C.1 voltage-imbalance** gains a `nema_hp_derate_pct` value linearly interpolated from the published NEMA MG-1 derate table (1% imbalance ~ 2% HP derate, 2% ~ 4%, 3% ~ 9%, 4% ~ 14%, 5% ~ 25% / do NOT operate). The full table is exported as `NEMA_HP_DERATE_TABLE` and returned in the result so the renderer can show the band the current reading falls into.

  2. **C.2 expansion-tank** gains `precharge_psi` (the air-side pre-charge value the tech sets at depressurized fill) and a `placement_note` ("Install on the suction side of the pump, at the supply main, before the first branch. Pre-charge the air side to the system fill pressure with the system depressurized.").

  3. **C.2 gas-pipe-sizing** gains `dP_achieved_in_wc` - the actual pressure drop at the chosen size and design load, derived from the Spitzglass sqrt(P) scaling: dP_actual = dP_design × (Q_actual / Q_max)^2. Lets the user see whether further regulation is needed without re-running the calc at a different design dP. Null when no candidate size satisfies the load.

  4. **C.3 manual-j-heating** now returns `tons` alongside `total_BTU_hr` (tons = total_BTU_hr / 12000). manual-j-cooling already returned tons; this brings parity. Heat-pump sizing reads in tons; gas furnaces in BTU/hr - showing both eliminates a mental conversion at the sizing decision.

  5. **C.5 dim-weight** gains `breakeven_in3` (the cubic-inch volume at which DIM equals actual weight: actual_weight × divisor), `current_in3` (the user's L × W × H), and a `billing_basis` flag ("DIM (cube-out)" vs "actual (weigh-out)"). Lets the shipper see the cross-over point at a glance.

  6. **C.5 brake-pad-life** accepts an optional `pad_set_cost_usd` and returns `cost_per_100k_miles_usd` = $/set × 100000 / miles_until_worn. Null when no $/set is supplied.

  7. **C.6 timber-cruise** accepts an optional `price_per_bf` and returns `value_usd` = bf × $/bf. Null when no price supplied. Doyle 14-inch / 16-foot log at $0.65/bf gives 100 bf × $0.65 = $65 stand value (regression-tested).

  16 new regression tests in test/unit/v8-phase-c-batch2.test.js across all seven refinements. 2199 unit tests passing total; lint clean; integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.4% of 100 KB; build 143 files / 1485 KB.

  v8 Phase C cumulative: 13 of ~30 spec §5 refinements landed across the two batches. Remaining ~17 are renderer-side polish (preset chips, list-row shorthand, climate-selector input mode, friction-rate color benchmarks, residential preset, full-job aggregations) best done one tile at a time.

- Phase C batch landed (spec-v8.md §5: per-tool UX refinements). Six high-leverage refinements across calc-electrical, calc-plumbing, calc-construction, and calc-mechanic. All six are compute-side additions consumed by existing renderers (no new tiles); each unlocks a follow-on UX wiring step the renderer can pick up at its convenience.

  1. **C.1 transformer-sizing** routed through the Phase D `roundToStandard(value, STANDARD_SIZES.transformer_kVA)` helper. The recommended next-standard kVA now comes from a single source of truth (the ANSI/IEEE C57 step series 15 / 30 / 45 / 75 / 112.5 / 150 / 225 / 300 / 500 / 750 / 1000 kVA) instead of the prior in-module list. Adds an `at_step_cap` boolean for loads exceeding 1000 kVA. Existing test updated: 100 kVA load now recommends 112.5 kVA (next ANSI step) instead of 100.

  2. **C.1 voltage-drop** gains companion outputs: `voltage_at_load_V` (source minus drop) and a `flag` string ("within advisory (≤3%)", "exceeds advisory (>3%)", "exceeds limit (>5%)") per NEC 210.19(A)(1) FPN 4 / 215.2(A)(1) FPN 2 advisory bands.

  3. **C.2 friction-loss** gains `velocity_ft_s` on both Hazen-Williams and Darcy-Weisbach branches (Hazen-Williams previously did not compute velocity), plus a `velocity_flag` ("within typical (≤5 ft/s)", "noise risk (>5 ft/s)", "erosion risk (>10 ft/s; copper especially)") matching engineering-practice plumbing thresholds.

  4. **C.4 concrete** gains `bags_60lb` and `bags_80lb` rollups computed from the with-waste cubic-foot total. Yields per Quikrete / Sakrete published values: 0.45 ft³ per 60 lb bag and 0.60 ft³ per 80 lb bag. The 80 lb bag count is always less than the 60 lb count (regression test).

  5. **C.5 displacement-cr** adds an explicit `requires_premium_octane` boolean flag at CR > 10.5:1, supplementing the existing `pump_gas_window` text. Lets the renderer surface a one-line callout without parsing the prose.

  6. **C.5 fuel-range** accepts an optional `price_per_gal` and returns `fuel_cost_usd` (tank × $/gal) and `cost_per_mile_usd` (cost / range_mi). Both fields are null when no $/gal is supplied (cost is never required, never persisted, never reported per spec §D.1).

  18 new regression tests in test/unit/v8-phase-c.test.js verifying each refinement against the spec thresholds (3% / 5% / 5 ft/s / 10 ft/s / 10.5:1 CR), step-series caps, exact-match passthroughs, and the optional-cost null-vs-supplied path. Phase D's three shared helpers (cost-output, context-band, standard-sizes) now have at least one in-the-wild caller (transformer-sizing uses standard-sizes; the rest are wired ad-hoc inline pending a future helper migration). 2183 unit tests passing total; lint clean; integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.4% of 100 KB; build 143 files / 1479 KB. Spec §5 lists ~30 per-tool refinements; six landed in this batch - the rest remain as follow-on per-tool PRs.

- Phase E.3 / E.4 / E.5 landed (spec-v8.md). Three more new utilities completing v8 Phase E (Phase E.2 trap-arm-length skipped as a duplicate of the existing v2 trap-arm tile per spec-v8 §7 "no new groups, no duplicates"). All three use the Phase D shared helpers (cost-output, context-band, standard-sizes) for follow-on cost wiring.

  1. **Utility 255 duct-leakage (Phase E.3) in calc-hvac.js.** SMACNA Duct Leakage Test Manual classes 3 / 6 / 12 / 24 / 48 (cfm per 100 ft^2 at 1 in WC). Computes leakage = design - measured CFM, normalizes to SMACNA reference via sqrt(P) orifice-flow scaling, returns leak-per-100-ft^2 + effective-class + pass/fail against the design class. Cites SMACNA Duct Leakage Test Manual (3rd ed.) and ASHRAE 90.1-2022 §6.4.4.2 by name.

  2. **Utility 256 residential-framing (Phase E.4) in calc-construction.js.** Stud + plate + joist + rafter rollup with board-feet totals from footprint, perimeter, wall height, joist span, rafter span, building run, and pitch. stud_count = ceil(perimeter / OC) + 8 corner/T allowance. plate_lf = ceil(perimeter × 3 × 1.10) (sole + 2 top + 10% waste). Rafter length uses the framing-square multiplier from utility 247. bf_per_ft for 2x4 / 2x6 / 2x8 / 2x10 / 2x12 lumber. Cites IRC 2021 Tables R502.5 / R602.5 / R802.5.1 + WWPA standard grading rules.

  3. **Utility 257 coagulant-dose (Phase E.5) in calc-water.js.** Pounds-formula equivalent for coagulant dosing: pure lb/day = MGD × mg/L × 8.34; product feed = pure / (strength %); product gal/day = product lb / (sg × 8.34). Manufacturer products: alum dry (100%, sg 1.0), alum liquid (48.5%, sg 1.33), ferric chloride (38%, sg 1.40), PAC (10%, sg 1.20). Cites Metcalf and Eddy 5th ed. + AWWA M37 by name.

- Phase A + Phase D foundation + Phase E.1 landed (spec-v8.md). Three discrete deliverables in one PR:

  1. **Phase A (manifest discipline lint).** `scripts/build-data.mjs` `buildAll` now writes an `asOf: TODAY` field into every per-folder manifest alongside the v6 `edition` stamp. New `scripts/check-manifests.mjs` runs as part of `npm run lint`: verifies that every `data/*/manifest.json` has `edition` (string) and `asOf` (ISO date), that every listed shard has a recorded hash, and future-proofs against `data/legal/*` per-entry `verifiedOn` drift (no-op today since no legal folder exists). 11 manifests refreshed in this PR; integrity unchanged at 96 entries.

  2. **Phase D (three shared helpers).** New `cost-output.js` exports `formatCost` (Intl.NumberFormat USD with two decimals) and `formatCostOutput(quantity, unitPrice, unitName)` (returns total + per-unit text or null on negative / non-finite inputs); plus `buildCostDisclosure` for the optional "Show cost" details/summary disclosure. New `context-band.js` exports `formatContextBand(value, low, high, unit)` (returns band: low / normal / high + booleans + display text "value unit (band; typical low-high unit)"; integer-vs-float aware). New `standard-sizes.js` exports `roundToStandard(value, sizes)` (returns recommended size, at_floor, at_cap flags) and `STANDARD_SIZES` map with five common ladders pre-populated: transformer_kVA (15 to 1000), breaker_amps (15 to 6000), pump_HP (0.25 to 100), water_heater_gal (40 to 100), service_amps (100 to 400). 23 unit tests in `test/unit/shared-helpers-v8.test.js` covering boundary conditions, ascending-sort validation, USD formatting, integer-float rendering, and error paths. All three modules added to `scripts/build.mjs` FILES and `sw.js` SHELL_ASSETS so production deploys ship them.

  3. **Phase E.1 (utility 254 panel-loading-rebalance).** New `panel-rebalance` tile in `calc-electrical.js`: per-phase totals + percent imbalance + greedy heaviest-to-lightest swap suggestion. Imbalance % = (max - min) / mean × 100. Swap suggestion fires when imbalance > 5 percent; iterates heavy-phase single-leg circuits sorted descending by amps and picks the first candidate that strictly reduces imbalance. Optional `swappable_pairs` constraint restricts the search to user-flagged breaker-position-compatible pairs. Cites NEC 2023 §220 + §408.36 + NEMA MG-1 by name. CITATIONS entry added with the spec §2.5 electrical governance variant. 10 unit tests in `test/unit/calc-electrical-v8.test.js`: balanced panel yields 0 imbalance and no suggestion; 30-30-0 forced-imbalance panel gives 75 percent (mean=40, max-min=30); suggestion always strictly improves imbalance; swappable_pairs constraint correctly excludes unlisted circuits; negative amps and unknown phase error.

  4. **Documentation.** `docs/derivations.md` gained section 48 (panel rebalance with the greedy-search algorithm and the 5 percent rebalance trigger).

- Step 60 complete (spec-v7.md): Group C v7 - HVAC extensions (utilities 242 through 245). Four new HVAC tiles in calc-hvac.js: duct-friction-static (utility 242: Darcy-Weisbach with Swamee-Jain explicit Colebrook approximation; round or rectangular ducts with Huebscher equivalent friction diameter D_eq = 1.30 x (W x H)^0.625 / (W + H)^0.250; absolute roughness from data/hvac/duct-roughness.json [galv smooth 0.0003 ft to flex metal 0.012 ft]; fitting losses from data/hvac/duct-fittings.json with 11 fitting types [elbow 90 smooth 0.22, tee thru-branch 1.30, etc.]; air density 0.075 lb/ft^3 / nu_air 1.62e-4 ft^2/s at 70 F sea level; total static = straight-duct + fitting losses), refrigerant-charging (utility 243: bundled manufacturer-attributed P-T tables for R-410A, R-32, R-454B, R-22 [legacy], R-134a in data/hvac/refrigerant-pt-tables.json; per-input psig vs psia toggle [psia = psig + 14.696]; superheat = T_line - T_sat[suction], subcool = T_sat[liquid] - T_line; manufacturer-typical 8-12 F superheat / 8-15 F subcool flags), cooling-tower (utility 244: range = T_in - T_out, approach = T_out - T_wb, heat rejection = gpm x 500 x range, fan kW per ton = fan_kW x 12000 / heat_rejection; flags 5-10 F approach / 8-12 F range as in-range), insulation-heat-loss (utility 245: cylindrical conduction Q = (T_s - T_a) / (R_cond + R_outside) where R_cond = ln(r2/r1) / (2 pi k); h_outside = h_conv(V_fpm) + h_rad(eps, T_s, T_a) iterated 12 fixed-point steps for the outer-surface coupling; six insulation types [fiberglass 0.025, mineral wool 0.026, calcium silicate 0.040, elastomeric 0.026, polyiso 0.018, phenolic foam 0.014 BTU-in / hr-ft^2-F]).

- v6 platform foundation (spec-v6.md §3 / §6 / §7). Five-piece foundation pass; per-group audit content lands in subsequent PRs (one per group, in the priority order from spec §6).

  1. **Edition stamps on every per-folder manifest.** `scripts/build-data.mjs` `DATASETS` table now carries an `edition` field per dataset; `buildAll` writes it into each `data/<folder>/manifest.json` and throws if any dataset is missing one. The eleven datasets are stamped: physical-constants ("NIST CODATA 2018"), electrical ("NEC 2023, IEEE 802.3bt-2018"), plumbing ("IPC 2021, IFGC 2021, AWWA M11 5th ed., USGS WSP-2339"), hvac ("ASHRAE 62.1-2022, ACCA Manual J 8th ed."), restoration ("IICRC S500/S520, August-Roche-Magnus"), construction ("IRC 2021, IBC 2021, ACI 211, ASCE 7, ASTM/SAE, AWS"), fire ("NFA hose-friction, ISO PPC"), crosswalks ("NIST SP 811, IRS 2024 mileage, GSA FY2026, NIOSH 1991, OSHA 29 CFR 1926"), summaries ("MIT-licensed creative work"), trucking ("FMCSA 49 CFR 395, 23 CFR 658.17, Thermo King / Carrier Transicold"), historical ("BLS PPI / EIA / USDA NASS / FRED, build-fetched daily").

  2. **Build-time prose-lint** (spec §2.3 / §7). `scripts/build-data.mjs` walks every shard body and flags string values longer than 140 characters that look like prose paste-ins. Per-key (`source`, `notes`, `attribution`, `summaries`, ...) and ancestor-aware (anything under a `summaries` parent object) exemptions cover the narrative shards (`summaries.json`, `v3-references.json`, etc.). Two latent values caught and exempted: the `iso_needed_fire_flow` formula gloss in `data/fire/fire-flow-formulas.json` and the per-tile entries inside `summaries/summaries.json` (the `wire-ampacity` summary, etc.). Build now logs "prose-lint clean; edition-stamp present on all manifests" on success.

  3. **`scripts/check-v6-discipline.mjs`** - standalone discipline-lint pass wired into `npm run lint`. Three checks: (a) edition-stamp lint verifies the on-disk manifest matches the build-pipeline rule (so a hand-edited manifest can't drop the field); (b) free-access lint cross-references every shipped shard against `docs/data-sources.md`, with wildcard support for fan-out shards (`### data/historical/commodities/*.json` matches every per-commodity file); (c) advisory citation-string lint counts inline `"per <Source>"` strings across every `calc-*.js` and prints the per-file count, telling the maintainer where the v6 audit work concentrates without blocking PRs that have not yet completed their group's audit. Initial run caught and fixed three missing entries in `docs/data-sources.md`: `niosh-coupling.json`, `heat-cold-stress.json`, `osha-trench.json`.

  4. **`docs/v6-audit.md`** - per-tile audit tracker. Carries the spec §6 checklist verbatim (reference block present in §3 order; edition or source date visible; free-access pointer named; governance notice from §2.5 sized to the stakes; numeric assumptions list source-stamped; "Copy answer with full reference block" wired; data shard prose-linted; docs/data-sources.md and scripts/sources.md entries up to date; data/integrity.json hash refreshed). Every group A through Q has its own status section and a per-tile table; the priority-1 Group A table marks all 25 electrical tiles "citation authored". Subsequent groups marked "not started". Document records the spec §6 priority order (electrical → plumbing → NFPA 13 → HVAC → IRC/IBC/AWC → FMCSA → FAA/USCG → FDA/USDA → AWWA → IICRC → everything else).

  5. **`citations.js`** - structured citation data model. Exports a `GOVERNANCE` map (the fifteen variants from spec §2.5: general / electrical / plumbing / structural / mechanical / fire / pesticide / trucking / aviation / marine / food / water / rigging / field / reference) and a `CITATIONS` map keyed by tile id. Each entry carries the six §3 fields (formula, edition, freeAccess, governance, editionNote, assumptions[]). Group A is the priority-1 worked example: 25 entries for ohms-law, wire-ampacity, voltage-drop, conduit-fill, box-fill, breaker-sizing, motor-fla, transformer-sizing, three-phase, copper-resistance, egc-sizing, service-load, generator-sizing, pv-string-sizing, battery-runtime, voltage-imbalance, gfci-afci-reference, lighting-density, pulling-tension, cable-bend-radius, pf-correction, phase-balance, multi-load-vd, lv-dc-drop, poe-budget. Each entry cites NEC by section number and edition only; no NEC table text is reproduced; numeric assumption lists name every constant the tile applies that the user does not enter (ambient, termination temperature, conductor count, fill-table column, voltage tolerance, etc.). The renderer `renderCitationBlock(parent, toolId)` mounts the six-line block beneath the result and is idempotent (replaces an existing block in the same parent). `buildAnswerWithReference(toolName, answerSummary, toolId)` builds the plain-text string the v3 "Copy citation" affordance becomes in v6: tool name, answer summary, formula, edition, free-access pointer, governance notice, edition note, and the assumption list as a bulleted block.

  6. **`app.js` integration.** When a tool view loads, the view dynamically imports `citations.js` and (a) mounts the §3 reference block under the existing `sources-region` if the tile has a structured citation entry, (b) appends a "Copy answer with full reference block" button that calls `clipboard.copyText(buildAnswerWithReference(...))`. Tiles not yet audited render exactly as before. The reference block is sized at the same scale as the answer per spec §8 (the reference is part of the answer); CSS picks up the existing dark / light / high-contrast theme and Big Buttons mode without per-rule changes.

  7. **Test coverage.** New `test/unit/citations.test.js` (11 tests): GOVERNANCE map covers every spec-§2.5 variant; every `CITATIONS` entry has the six required §3 fields and only valid governance values; Group A audit coverage check parses `app.js` for every Group A tile id and asserts a `CITATIONS` entry exists; `buildAnswerWithReference` paths cover missing entries, present entries (formula / edition / free-access / governance / assumptions), an NEC-edition string in the voltage-drop output, and the omit-assumptions-when-empty rule; `renderCitationBlock` paths return null on unknown tile id, mount a `.v6-reference-block` with the formula and assumption rows, and replace an existing block on a second call. 1838 unit tests passing total; lint clean (edition stamps + free-access doc coverage); home-view payload 37.6% of 100 KB budget after the new module joins the SHELL_ASSETS list (citations.js is shell-cached, lazy-loaded by app.js on first tool view).

  Per spec §6, v6 is "done" only when every tile is `complete` in `docs/v6-audit.md`. The platform pass landed here unblocks the per-group audit PRs; the next PR picks up Group B (plumbing / IPC / IFGC, priority 2) and so on through priority 11.

### UX polish

- Brand mark and tab title relabeled: index.html `<title>` from "roughlogic - field math for the trades" to "Rough Logic"; changelog.html `<title>` from "roughlogic - changelog" to "Rough Logic - Changelog"; visible header brand `wordmark` from "roughlogic" to "Rough Logic" (the visible "field math for the trades." tagline span removed); site.webmanifest `name` and `short_name` to "Rough Logic" so the PWA install card matches.

- Section labels on the home grid drop the "Group A" / "Group B" prefix and now read just the category name (`Electrical`, `Plumbing and Gas`, `HVAC`, `Water Damage and Mold Restoration`, `Carpentry and Construction`, `Fire-Ground Engineering`, `Cross-Trade Utilities`, `Knowledge References`). The per-tile group tag mirrors the change. Internal `tool.group` letters (A-H) and the `data-group` attribute stay so URL filtering and CSS hooks are unaffected.

- Search bar now has tool-name autocomplete via a native `<datalist id="tool-suggestions">` populated at boot from the live `TOOLS` registry. Typing matches against every tool name; picking a suggestion that exactly matches a tool name routes the user straight to that tool view (no extra click). Empty queries and partial substrings continue to drive the live home-grid filter exactly as before. Search-input placeholder swapped from "Search 119 tools" (stale) to "Search tools".

### Build progress (v4)

- Step 55 complete (spec-v4.md): Group P - Field, Backcountry, and SAR (utilities 227-232). New calc-field.js with `computePacing` (calibration-based pace length with terrain factor flat/rolling/steep/brush/snow plus a quick-reference table per stride length), `computeBearingConversion` (magnetic <-> true with east-is-least / west-is-best memo, 0-360 normalization), `computeSlopeAvalanche` (rise/run or measured angle, slope %, 30-45 deg avalanche start-zone window flag), `computeBackcountryNeeds` (water L/day from cool/moderate/hot/extreme bands, kcal/day from easy/moderate/hard/extreme exertion factor, trip totals scaled by days and group size), `computeUTM` with full Krueger forward and inverse Lat/Lon <-> UTM (WGS84) - round-trip Denver lat/lon -> UTM zone 13N -> lat/lon verified to 4 decimal places, and `computeSolarTimes` implementing the public NOAA solar-position algorithm (sunrise, sunset, civil/nautical/astronomical twilight, declination, equation of time; verified against Denver summer-solstice yielding ~14.9 hours daylight and equator equinox yielding ~12 hours). Six renderers added; UTM uses a bespoke renderer to handle the bidirectional input mode. Tools registered in TOOLS group P (`Field, Backcountry, and SAR`); `field` added to TRADES; `P` added to GROUPS. 60 new unit tests in test/unit/calc-field.test.js.

- Step 54 complete (spec-v4.md): Group O - Kitchen and Food Service (utilities 222-226). New calc-kitchen.js with `computeRecipeScale` (linear scale by target/original yield with USDA reference-weight conversion to grams when fractional eggs or unusual cup amounts arise; ingredient densities for flour, sugar, butter, milk, oil, honey, rice, oats), `computeYieldEP` (yield % = EP/AP * 100; EP cost per lb = AP cost / yield), `computeCoolingCurve` (FDA Food Code 2022 135 F -> 70 F in <= 2 hr and 70 F -> 41 F in <= 4 hr with container, product type, and ambient adjustment; pass/fail flags), `computePlateCost` (plate cost, suggested menu price = cost / target food cost %, contribution margin, sanity flag), and `computePanConversion` (pan capacity in qt, pans needed, servings per pan from full / two-thirds / half / third / quarter / sixth / ninth pan sizes at 2.5 / 4 / 6 inch depth; cooling-depth warning at depth >= 4 in cross-references utility 224). Five renderers added; recipe scaling and plate cost use bespoke list-based renderers. Tools registered in TOOLS group O (`Kitchen and Food Service`); `kitchen` added to TRADES; `O` added to GROUPS. 50 new unit tests in test/unit/calc-kitchen.test.js.

- Step 53 complete (spec-v4.md): Group N - Stage and Live Production (utilities 216-221). New calc-stage.js with `computeTrussCapacity` (manufacturer-attributed UDL curves for 12-inch box, 16-inch box, 20.5-inch ladder; equivalent-UDL safety factor with 2x point-load rule of thumb; reactions A/B from simple-beam math), `computeTimeAlignment` (speed of sound c = 331.3 + 0.606 * T_C, delay-tower delay in ms, Haas-window 10-30 ms offset), `computeDMX` (per-fixture channel ranges, universe utilization %, conflict and overflow detection, split-recommendation flag), `computeNeutralImbalance` (I_N = sqrt(I_A^2 + I_B^2 + I_C^2 - I_A*I_B - I_B*I_C - I_A*I_C) with harmonic-load warning; companion to v3 utility 128), `computeSPL` (L2 = L1 - 20 log10(d2/d1) with free-field / hemispherical / indoor mode adjustment), and `computeRiggingCheck` (WLL at angle for shackles / slings / span sets / hoists; choker derate 0.75 matches v3 utility 161). Six renderers added; truss-capacity and DMX use bespoke list-based renderers. Tools registered in TOOLS group N (`Stage and Live Production`); `stage` added to TRADES; `N` added to GROUPS. 60 new unit tests in test/unit/calc-stage.test.js. After Steps 53-55: 1802 unit tests passing; lint clean; data:verify clean (66 entries / 56 shards / 10 datasets); home-view payload 36.6% of 100 KB budget.

- Step 50 complete (spec-v4.md): Group K - Mechanic, Auto / Marine / Aviation (utilities 195-202). New calc-mechanic.js with `computeWeightBalance` (CG = total moment / total weight against AFM CG and gross limits, FAA AC 91-23A cited by name only), `computePropSlip` (theoretical kt = (RPM/gear) * pitch / 1056; planing 10-15% vs displacement 25-30% category), `computeDisplacementCR` (displacement in^3/L and static compression ratio = (V_cyl + V_TDC) / V_TDC with V_TDC = chamber + gasket + deck - dome), `computeBoltStretch` (clamp load F = (stretch * area * E) / grip across steel/stainless/inconel/titanium/aluminum), `computeDriveshaftCritical` (Euler-Bernoulli first-mode N_crit = (4.7/L^2) * sqrt((EI)/(rho*A)) with 0.65x recommended max), `computeFuelRange` (BTU and kWh from tank * LHV, range from tank * mpg * load factor across gasoline E10/E85, diesel #2, LPG, CNG, jet A), `computeTireGearing` (parses metric 285/75R17 and imperial 33x12.50R17 sizes; rev/mi, effective ratio, recommended axle ratio from candidate set 3.73 / 4.10 / 4.56 / 4.88 / 5.13 / 5.38), and `computeBrakePadLife` (KE = 0.5 m v^2, rotor temp rise, wear-rate by organic/semi-metallic/ceramic). Eight renderers added. Tools registered in TOOLS group K (`Mechanic - Auto, Marine, Aviation`); `mechanic` added to TRADES; `K` added to GROUPS. 82 new unit tests in test/unit/calc-mechanic.test.js including 350 SBC ish 5.7 L sanity, KE-from-mass-and-velocity verification, and tire-size parser round-trip. After Steps 50-52: 1629 unit tests passing; data:verify clean (66 entries / 56 shards / 10 datasets); home-view payload 35.2% of 100 KB.

### Build progress (v3)

- Step 47 complete (spec-v3.md): Group I v3 - Field Notes scratchpad and Crash-Safe Resume (utilities 185, 187). Utility 185: a 280-character textarea per tool view that mounts under the calculator and binds to the URL hash key `k=`. Typing debounces 200 ms then `history.replaceState`s the new hash so the back button is not polluted by every keystroke. Notice under the textarea: "Notes are stored in the URL only. Closing the tab without bookmarking discards them." `routing.js` already parses arbitrary query params via `URLSearchParams`, so `params.k` rehydrates the textarea on a bookmarked load with no parser changes. Utility 187: `renderToolView` now wraps the renderer body and the post-mount support-libs in a try/catch boundary. On uncaught error, log `{ tool, params, error }` to console and mount a `.crash-panel` `role="alert"` reading "This calculator crashed. Reload to retry, or paste your URL into a new tab to recover state. The URL is preserved." The hash is intentionally untouched so the user can recover. New `.scratchpad-region` and `.crash-panel` CSS in styles.css; print stylesheet keeps the scratchpad visible (with a 1px black border) and hides the URL-only notice line. Utility 186 (Send To Other Device) deferred until utility 181 QR is implemented (Step 45). Note: skipping the QR step for now because the bundled MIT QR library is non-trivial and would push the home payload past the budget if not dynamic-imported; will revisit.

- Step 46 complete (spec-v3.md): Group I v3 - Big Buttons mode and High-Contrast theme (utilities 182, 183). theme.js rewritten to support a 3-way theme cycle (`dark` -> `light` -> `high-contrast` -> `dark`) keyed off the existing `rl-theme` localStorage key, plus a Big Buttons mode keyed off a new `rl-bigbuttons` localStorage key (both keys are explicitly blessed by the v3 spec section 1). High-contrast palette: pure black surfaces (`#000000`), pure white text, 2px white borders on every panel, and a high-visibility yellow focus ring (`#ffff00`); WCAG AAA contrast across all text. Big Buttons mode bumps `--touch-min` from 48 px to 64 px, font size 1.125x, input/button heights to 64 px, and tile padding up. Both toggles wired in `<head>` before first paint to avoid flicker. New `<button id="big-buttons-toggle" class="theme-toggle big-buttons-toggle">Big</button>` in the header next to the existing theme toggle; pressed state inverts color. Numpad layout toggle (utility 184) deferred - current `inputmode="decimal"` already gives every number field a numeric soft keyboard on mobile; a separate phone/calculator layout selector adds UI weight without obvious payoff. Will revisit if a user asks. 1344 unit tests still passing; home-view payload 33.0% of 100 KB.

- Step 39 complete (spec-v3.md): Group C v3 - HVAC Round Three (utilities 139 through 144). - Step 38 complete (spec-v3.md): Group B v3 - Plumbing and Gas Round Three (utilities 132 through 138). Added `computeStormwaterRational` (Q = C * i * A with bundled coefficients per surface; cfs and gpm), `computeManningSlope` (English Manning V = (1.486/n) * R^(2/3) * S^(1/2) solved for self-cleansing slope at 2 ft/s and the slope to carry target flow at half-full with R = D/4), `computeHydrostaticTest` (test pressure 1.5x water / 1.25x gas with optional override; piecewise hold-time recommendation), `computeGreaseTrap` (volume = peak_gpm * retention * loading_factor; PDI G101 cited; recommended nominal from a 14-step ladder), `computeGlycolMix` (linear interpolation across manufacturer freeze-point curves for propylene and ethylene; concentrate gallons), `computeExpansionTank` (V_tank = V_sys * ((rho_cold/rho_hot) - 1) / (1 - P_i/P_f) with absolute pressures and a public water-density table), and `computeBackflowLoss` (linear interpolation of manufacturer pressure-loss curves by device class and pipe size) in calc-plumbing.js. Seven renderers added. Tools registered in TOOLS, TOOL_MODULES, TOOL_DATA_SOURCES (stormwater-rational, manning-slope, glycol-mix, backflow-loss data-driven). Home-view payload 27.5% of 100 KB budget.

- Step 37 complete (spec-v3.md): Group A v3 - Electrical Round Three (utilities 125 through 131). Added `computePullingTension` (capstan equation T_out = T_in * exp(mu * theta) accumulated per bend, sidewall pressure T/R per bend, head-end and sidewall flags against 5000 lb / 1000 lb-per-ft thresholds), `computeBendRadius` (manufacturer-attributed multiples of cable OD: THHN/XHHW 8x, MC 7x, control 6x, coax 10x, fiber 20x), `computePFCorrection` (kVAR = kW * (tan(acos(PF1)) - tan(acos(PF2))); microfarads from Q = V^2 * 2*pi*f*C at 60 Hz with three-phase Y per-leg form), `computePhaseBalance` (per-phase totals, imbalance percent over average, greedy heaviest-to-lightest swap suggestion), `computeMultiLoadVoltageDrop` (cumulative I*R per segment along ordered loads, single-phase round-trip), `computeLVDCDrop` (12/24/48 V DC drop with application-tolerance flag table: LED 3%, marine 10%, marine-critical 3%, RV 5%, audio 2%), and `computePoEBudget` (IEEE 802.3 af/at/bt3/bt4 budgets, Cat5e/6/6A loop resistance with copper-alpha temperature correction, green/amber/red flag against per-class PD minimum) in calc-electrical.js. Home-view payload 27.0% of 100 KB budget (calc-electrical.js loads on first electrical-tool view via dynamic-import).

### Repo cleanup for public release

- Repo audited and cleaned for public release. Deleted: `encryptalotta/` (a 3.6 MB foreign git repo accidentally nested inside roughlogic-dev during the theme-port reference work), `logo.jpg` (178 KB brand source; the favicon.svg shipped at runtime is the live brand mark), `.eslintrc.json` (no npm script invokes ESLint; the lint contract is grep + n-gram + home-payload checks), `dist/` (build output; regenerated by `npm run build`), and `test-results/` / `playwright-report/` (Playwright failure artifacts; regenerated each run). `scripts/grep-checks.mjs` `TOKEN_CHECK_SKIP` no longer references the removed `.eslintrc.json`. `.gitignore` extended to explicitly cover `test-results/`, `playwright-report/`, and the `probe-tmp.mjs` interactive-development files. `scripts/derivations.md` index updated to list all 24 derivations (v1 1-11 + v2 12-24) instead of the v1-only list. Repo size dropped from 29 MB to 20 MB; the deployable surface (everything not gitignored) is even smaller.

- Real silently-broken behavior fixed: arrow-key tile navigation. The keyboard handler in `bindShortcuts()` did `getElementById("tile-grid")` and skipped wiring when null. The v2 render-by-group system replaced the single `<ul id="tile-grid">` with `<div id="tools-sections">` containing N `<ul class="tile-grid">` (one per group A through H), so `tile-grid` as an id no longer existed and arrow-key navigation was silently inert from the v2 expansion onward. Re-pointed the listener at `#tools-sections` (with a fallback to `#tile-grid` for any future reversion); the inner `querySelectorAll(".tile-link")` already walks every `<ul class="tile-grid">` block in document order so Tab + Arrow-Right traverses tiles across group boundaries seamlessly. Verified end-to-end in real Chromium: focusing Ohm's Law (Group A tile 1), pressing ArrowRight focuses Wire Ampacity (Group A tile 2); ArrowDown focuses Box Fill (Group A tile 5, row 2). New integration regression guard "Arrow-key navigation works across v2 group sections" added; 45 / 45 integration tests pass.

- One dead CSS class removed: `.tile.is-hidden { display: none; }`. With the v2 render-by-group system, filtered-out tiles are simply not rendered into the DOM (renderHome iterates groups and only appends tiles that pass `matchesFilters`); the `is-hidden` class was never added to a tile by JS. Confirmed by a node script that grep'd every CSS class against HTML + every JS file in the repo: only one class (`is-hidden`) had zero references outside CSS itself. Removed.

- README "Quick start" tightened: "Select a tool" replaced with "Click the tile to open the calculator", reflecting the new card-link behavior where the entire tile body is clickable (not just the small "Open tool" button).

- Card-link Cmd/Ctrl-click opens the tool in a new tab. Previously the tile click handler returned early on any modifier-key click (Cmd / Ctrl / Shift / middle-click), so power users could not multi-pop tools without using the explicit "Open tool" anchor's right-click menu. Now Cmd/Ctrl-click on the tile body calls `window.open(href, "_blank", "noopener")` to open the tool in a new tab; Shift / middle-click still skip (matching the explicit-link semantics where Shift opens in a new window and middle-click is browser-handled). Verified end-to-end in real Chromium: Cmd-click on the title area of "Ohm's Law" opens `#ohms-law` in a new tab while the original tab stays on home.

- Card-link UX pattern: the entire tile body is now clickable. Previously only the explicit "Open tool" link inside each tile was clickable - clicking the title, description, tags, or whitespace did nothing. encryptalotta makes the whole card a button; roughlogic now matches. styles.css adds `cursor: pointer` to `.tile` and `position: relative; z-index: 2` to `.tile-pin` so the Pin button stays separately interactive. app.js `buildTile` adds a `click` handler on the LI that calls `navigateTo(tool.id)` unless the click landed on `.tile-pin` (own handler), `.tile-link` (native href navigation), modifier-key clicks (Cmd/Ctrl/Shift = open in new tab), or middle-click. End-to-end verified in real Chromium: click in title area opens the tool, Pin click toggles state without navigating, "Open tool" link click navigates as before. New integration regression guard "entire tile body is clickable (card-link pattern), Pin stays separate" added; 44 / 44 integration tests pass.

Both run in parallel after the lint+unit+data-integrity job. Comment headers added to ci.yml documenting what each job covers.

- `npm run test:e2e` and `npm run test:a11y` were byte-identical commands - both ran the same Playwright config which runs all 43 tests. Split per spec section 13's two named test passes: `test:e2e` continues to run the full integration suite (43 tests; axe-core routes + smoke + layout + theme + viewer), while `test:a11y` now runs only the 27 axe-core route scans via `--grep 'a11y:'`. CI workflows that want a fast pre-merge a11y signal without the smoke overhead can now invoke `npm run test:a11y` (about 9 seconds, was 16 seconds for the full suite). Both scripts honor the same playwright.config.js webServer setup and the same test file.

(2) The import line `import { parseHashRoute, decodePinnedList, decodeIdList, toolMatches } from "./routing.js"` brought in `decodePinnedList` and `decodeIdList` neither of which app.js uses anymore (parseHashRoute decodes the lists internally) - import line trimmed to `{ parseHashRoute, toolMatches }`. - Keyboard-Enter activation regression guard. The brand link and back-link no-scroll-to-top fix lives in a `click` event handler. Browsers fire `click` for both pointer-click and Enter on a focused anchor, so the fix is meant to apply to keyboard activation too. New integration test "Brand link and back-link route home via keyboard Enter without scroll-to-top" focuses each link, presses Enter, and asserts `window.scrollY === 0` and `#tools` is visible afterward. 41 / 41 integration tests pass.

- Brand link and "Back to tools" link no longer cause a scroll-to-top jump before routing home. Both used `href="#"` so the browser's default click handling scrolled to the document top *before* the hashchange handler routed home and rewrote the URL. Visible as a brief jump on every navigation back to home from a tool view. Now both links bind a click handler that calls `e.preventDefault()` and then `navigateTo("")` directly. The `href="#"` is kept so right-click "Open in new tab" still works (modifier keys / middle-click bypass the preventDefault). Verified end-to-end in real Chromium: clicking brand or back-link from a tool view leaves `scrollY=0`, swaps to home, and writes `#r=<recent-tool>` to the URL with no intermediate scroll-to-top frame.

No JS errors anywhere. The "frame-ancestors ignored in <meta>" warning is gone after the recent cleanup. Static deploy via Cloudflare Pages from the dist/ directory remains the deployment model, with no server-side runtime, no cross-origin fetches, and no third-party domains.

- Real CSS specificity bug found and fixed: the HTML `hidden` attribute was being silently overridden by author CSS. When `clipboard.js`'s `addCopyAllButton` injected a Copy-all button on a Group H reference utility (e.g., `#color-codes`), it correctly set `btn.hidden = true` because reference views render `<dl>` lists with no labelled `<p>` rows for the button to act on. But `.copy-all-btn { display: inline-flex }` in author CSS outranked the user-agent `[hidden] { display: none }` rule by specificity, so the button stayed visible despite `hidden=true`. Verified end-to-end against dist/: Copy-all button rendered on every reference page with text "Copy all" but no labels under it. Fix: added a top-level `[hidden] { display: none !important }` so the `hidden` attribute always wins regardless of component-level `display` declarations. Now Copy-all is correctly hidden on `#color-codes` and correctly visible on `#voltage-drop` after its example button populates 2 labelled output rows. The same fix benefits any other element with a `display:` rule and an `el.hidden` toggle: the offline pill (currently not in DOM but the rule was vulnerable), the empty-state notice, the recents/pinned regions, and `<noscript>` blocks.

- Two new integration regression guards covering the above. `test/integration/a11y.test.js` adds: "Copy-all button stays hidden on Group H reference views" (loads #color-codes, asserts btn.count() === 1 and isVisible() === false), and "Copy-all button is visible on a calculator with labelled outputs" (loads #voltage-drop, clicks the example button, asserts the Copy-all button is now visible). 37 / 37 integration tests pass.
