- Search bar now auto-routes to home when typed from a tool view. Previously, if a user was inside a calculator (e.g., #voltage-drop) and started typing in the persistent header search bar, `state.query` updated and `renderHome()` ran, but the home view was hidden so nothing visible changed. To see filtered results they had to manually navigate back to home. `bindSearch()` now detects when the user is on a tool view and the new query is non-empty, and calls `navigateTo("")` which swaps to the home view and shows the filtered grid. Empty queries do not auto-navigate (typing then clearing the field should not yank the user out of a calculator). Verified end-to-end: from #voltage-drop, typing "ohm" hides the view-region, shows the tools section, filters to 2 matching tiles, URL becomes "#r=voltage-drop" (recent tool preserved). 34/34 integration tests still pass.

- Header theme-toggle integration test stabilized. The "header theme toggle touch target is at least 48x48 pixels" test was passing in isolation but intermittently failing in the parallel run. Cause: the header's `rl-fade-down` keyframe briefly translates the element 8 px above the viewport top, so `boundingBox()` returns the visible-clipped portion (height 40 px) until the keyframe settles. Added a 600 ms `waitForTimeout` so the test measures the resting position. Verified deterministic across three back-to-back full integration runs (34/34 each time).

- Spurious "frame-ancestors ignored" console warning silenced on every page load. Both index.html and changelog.html shipped a `<meta http-equiv="Content-Security-Policy">` that included `frame-ancestors 'none'` - but that directive is HTTP-header-only by CSP spec and is silently ignored when delivered via meta. Browsers logged "The Content Security Policy directive 'frame-ancestors' is ignored when delivered via a <meta> element." on every load (visible in earlier Playwright probes). Dropped `frame-ancestors 'none'` from both meta tags. The production `_headers` file still carries it (correctly delivered via HTTP), so clickjacking protection is unchanged. scripts/dev.mjs already serves the directive via the HTTP CSP header, so local dev parity is preserved. Verified end-to-end: page loads with zero console warnings.

- Three real bugs surfaced and fixed by running the full Playwright + axe-core integration suite end-to-end.

  1. **playwright.config.js webServer cwd bug.** The webServer command `npx -y http-server -p 8080 -c-1 .` was resolving `.` from `test/integration/`, not the repo root. Every page request 404'd; every a11y test was nominally "passing" only because `axe.analyze()` against an empty page produced an empty violations array. Added `cwd: "../.."` to anchor http-server at the repo root. Reproduced, confirmed the fix.

  2. **Animation-induced WCAG 2 AA contrast failures across all 27 axe routes.** The `rl-fade-down` (header) and `rl-fade-up` (view-region) keyframes ramped opacity from 0 to 1 over 0.5 / 0.4 seconds. axe-core sampled the page mid-animation and saw text composited at sub-full opacity (white-on-white at ~85% effective opacity, apparent foreground `#cbcbcb` on `#ffffff` -> 1.62:1) -> "color-contrast" violation, "serious" impact, on every route. Rewrote both keyframes to animate `transform` only; elements render at full contrast at every frame. The motion is preserved for users who want it; `prefers-reduced-motion` still disables it entirely.

  3. **Stale integration tests.** `test/integration/a11y.test.js` "filter buttons toggle aria-pressed" and "touch targets are at least 48x48 pixels" both targeted DOM elements that were removed (the trade/group filter row). Replaced with five tests that exercise the actual current DOM: theme toggle flips data-theme and persists across reloads (covers the rl-theme localStorage round-trip), home tile-link 48 px touch target, header theme-toggle 48x48 touch target, search-input narrows tile count when typed into, home renders all eight group sections.

  Final integration result: 34 of 34 Playwright + axe-core tests passing (was 27 phantom-passing on an empty page; now genuinely passing on the rendered v1 + v2 surface).

- Final pass to reconcile every "no localStorage" claim with the theme.js usage. Five remaining inaccuracies updated: README.md "Safety guarantees" line ("Read-only by default ... does not write to localStorage..."), spec.md section 7 ("No localStorage, sessionStorage, cookies, or IndexedDB. The service worker cache is the only client-side persistence."), spec.md section 11.5 ("URL hash carries pinned-tile state and calculator input state. No localStorage, no cookies."), docs/launch-checklist.md row "No localStorage / sessionStorage / cookies / IndexedDB | pass | None used.", and docs/launch-checklist.md v0.2.0 deploy-time-gates "Behavior" line. Each rewritten to state precisely what is and is not stored: localStorage holds one key (`rl-theme`, value `"light"` or `"dark"`); no sessionStorage, cookies, or IndexedDB; the URL hash remains the only state mechanism for tool data. docs/threat-model.md T11 wording also tightened. The project's contract now matches its code across spec.md, README.md, all four docs/ files, and CHANGELOG.

- app.js dead-code cleanup. After the trade/group filter row and the offline pill came out of index.html, `state.trade` / `state.group` were never written but were still threaded through `matchesFilters` -> `routing.toolMatches` on every keystroke, and the orphaned `bindFilters()` and `bindOfflinePill()` functions sat in source as un-called code. Dropped both fields from `state`, simplified `matchesFilters` to `toolMatches(tool, { query: state.query })`, and removed the two function definitions. `routing.toolMatches` itself keeps full trade/group support (defaulted to "all" when absent) so the routing.test.js suite continues to pass. Verified in real Chromium: 119 tiles render, search filters down to 1 tile when typing "ohm", no JS errors. Home-view payload edges down from 25.3% to 25.1% of the 100 KB budget.

- Boot path tightened. `boot()` no longer calls `bindFilters()` (the trade/group filter row was removed from index.html), `bindOfflinePill()` (the offline pill was removed from the footer), or the idle-deferred dynamic import of `data-stamp.js` for `stampFooterVersion()` (the data-version footer line was removed). All three were silent no-ops because the underlying DOM elements no longer exist; the third was actually fetching `data-stamp.js` on every cold home-view load just to call a function that returned immediately. - 48 px touch-target floor restored on every interactive element per spec.md section 11.6 / spec-v2.md section 1. After the encryptalotta theme port, several controls had drifted below the spec floor: `.tile-link` (40 px), `.tile-pin` (40 px), `.theme-toggle` (40 x 40 px square), `.copy-btn` / `.copy-all-btn` (no min-height; rendered around 28-30 px), `.filter-btn` for the "Clear recents" / "Clear pins" pill (36 px). Each promoted to `min-height: var(--touch-min)` (48 px) with horizontal padding bumped where needed to keep the visual pill shape. - Light-mode WCAG AA fix for invalid-input and integrity-banner colors. The dark-mode validity reds (border `#ff5d6c`, reason text `#ff8c95`) read 2.99:1 and 2.23:1 on white - both fail WCAG AA's 4.5:1 minimum for body text. Promoted both colors to CSS variables (`--error-border`, `--error-text`) and added a light-mode override using `#c0392b` (5.4:1 on white) and `#a93226` (6.6:1 on white). Dark-mode behavior unchanged: same `#ff5d6c` border and `#ff8c95` reason text. The integrity-banner red border now also flows through the variable, so a tampered-data warning stays readable in either theme.

- Documentation reconciled with the theme.js localStorage usage. docs/threat-model.md T7 (Privacy leakage) updated from a blanket "no localStorage" claim to a precise statement that localStorage is used for one key (`rl-theme`, value `"light"` or `"dark"`) for theme persistence and nothing else; no calculator inputs, pinned set, recents ring, or bundle data is written there. docs/architecture.md "Persistence" section reconciled the same way. Both documents continue to assert the URL hash as the only state mechanism for tool data.

- scripts/check-home-payload.mjs now counts theme.js toward the 100 KB home-view first-paint budget. theme.js is loaded synchronously from `<head>` so it runs before the first paint to apply the saved theme without flicker; treating it as part of first-paint cost is honest. Payload total grows from 23.5 KB to 25.6 KB (25.0% of the 100 KB budget); ample headroom remains.

- theme.js (light/dark toggle) now ships to dist/ via scripts/build.mjs SHELL_FILES copy list. Previously theme.js existed at the repo root and was referenced by index.html / changelog.html `<script src="theme.js">` and by sw.js shell precache, but the build manifest didn't include it - so the deployed Cloudflare Pages copy was missing the file, which 404'd on every page load and silently left the theme toggle wired to nothing. theme.js also added to scripts/grep-checks.mjs TARGETS (passes the innerHTML / eval / em-dash / emoji audit). Verified end-to-end against the dist/ build served by `python3 -m http.server`: 119 tiles in 8 sections render, theme toggle flips `<html data-theme>` between `light` (body bg `#ffffff`) and `dark` (`#0a0a0a`) with zero JS errors. dist/ count grows from 79 to 80 files.

- styles.css rewritten to mirror encryptalotta.com's dark "delightful" theme. Same near-black layered surfaces (`#0a0a0a` page, `#1a1a1a` cards, `#2a2a2a` inputs), white-on-dark text with two muted secondary tints (`#c8c8c8` 8.5:1 and `#9a9a9a` 5.5:1 on the card background to keep WCAG AA), Apple-system font stack, sticky topbar with backdrop blur, rounded tile cards (240 px min, 14 px radius) with a small `->` arrow that fades in on hover, white pill buttons that go dark on hover, pill-shaped Tag chips and footer badges, gentle fade-up entry animations, and a `prefers-reduced-motion` opt-out. Every existing class name preserved (`.tile`, `.tile-grid`, `.filter-btn`, `.view-region`, `.view-pin`, `.view-share`, `.view-bundle-*`, `.view-print`, `.view-bundle-load`, `.pinned-header`, `.offline-pill`, `.copy-btn`, `.copy-all-btn`, `.integrity-banner`, `.inline-notice`, `.citation`, `.data-source-stamp`, `.tile-link`, `.tile-pin`, `.skip-link`, `.visually-hidden`, `#changelog-content` headings) so app.js and the calculator modules render unchanged. Touch targets remain 48 px; focus rings are a clear blue (`#4d90fe`) outline; the print stylesheet now flips back to white-on-black for ink. index.html / changelog.html / site.webmanifest updated to `color-scheme: dark` and `theme_color #0a0a0a` so the browser chrome and PWA install card match. Home-view payload after gzip: 23 KB / 100 KB (22.7% of budget). 839 unit tests still passing; lint and data:verify clean.

- 3 new unit tests in test/unit/build-sw-patch.test.js asserting the spec.md section 6 cache-name invariant: source sw.js retains the `dev-*` placeholder so local-dev caching works without a build, dist/sw.js (when present) has a 15-char `YYYYMMDDTHHMMSS` BUILD_HASH (no longer the placeholder), and dist/sw.js cache names include the BUILD_HASH constant. Tests skip cleanly in environments where dist/ has not been built yet (e.g. fresh CI checkout before the build step). 839 unit tests passing.

- Service worker cache name now keyed by build hash per spec.md section 6 ("Cache name includes the build hash; old caches are deleted on activation"). Previously sw.js shipped with a literal `dev-0001` placeholder so every deploy reused the same cache name; old caches were only deleted when the file list changed *and* the SW re-installed, which is a fragile invariant. scripts/build.mjs now reads the build timestamp and patches `const BUILD_HASH = "YYYYMMDDTHHMMSS";` into the shipped dist/sw.js (ISO 8601 basic format, second precision, 15 chars; e.g. `20260505T204419`). Each release thus produces unique `roughlogic-shell-<hash>` and `roughlogic-data-<hash>` cache names; the existing activate-time keys-difference cleanup deletes prior caches automatically. The build fails fast if the BUILD_HASH constant cannot be located in the source sw.js (a pattern-mismatch guard against future refactors). The source sw.js retains the `dev-0001` placeholder so local-dev caching still works without a build step.

- Tool count corrected from 118 to 119 across user-facing copy. Spec-v2.md authored utilities 65 through 118 (54 new); a follow-on landed utility 119 (Compare Two Refrigerants) implemented under Group C per spec-v2 Step 31. - scripts/analyze-data-changes.mjs taught the v2 shard shapes. The data-refresh PR-body generator drilled into v1 layers (values, rates, refrigerants, summaries) but treated v2 shards (charge_per_foot, equivalent-lengths, insulation, hepa-loading, soil-bearing, wind-snow-zones, irs-mileage, gsa-perdiem, demand-factors, lighting-density, material-expansion, septic-rules, v2-references) as opaque top-level objects, so a value change inside one of them surfaced as a generic shard-changed entry instead of a per-key added/removed/modified report. Also documents that `#b=...` takes precedence over a `#p=...` form so a bundle URL is never silently demoted. 836 unit tests passing.

- Project Bundle (utility 121) now encodes inputs for *every* calculator visited this session, not only the active one. - Step 32 complete (spec-v2.md): Group I - Project Bundle (utility 121). New bundle.js exports encodeBundle / encodeBundleHash / decodeBundle / sanitizeBundle. Bundle shape is `{ version: 1, pinned: [...ids], recents: [...ids], inputs: { [toolId]: { ...key/value } } }`. URL hash form is `#b=<base64url-JSON>` (32 KB cap, malformed-input rejection). routing.js parseHashRoute exposes `bundle` for the `b=` form; app.js parseHash decodes asynchronously, sanitizes against the live tool registry, and replaces the bundle hash with the resolved p=...&r=... form. Tool view header gains three new actions: "Copy bundle URL" (encodes current state + the active calculator's input map and copies to clipboard), "Download bundle" (creates a same-origin Blob URL and triggers an anchor download), and "Load bundle" (file input that decodes and replays via state and navigateTo("")). Bundle inputs auto-merge into the renderer's params on tool open. CSP unchanged; Blob URLs are same-origin. New test/unit/bundle.test.js with 18 cases (round-trip, malformed JSON, malformed base64url, version mismatch, size cap, sanitize against live ids, etc.); 802 unit tests passing.

- Step 30 complete (spec-v2.md): Group H - Knowledge References (utilities 114 through 118) in the new calc-references.js. - Step 29 complete (spec-v2.md): Group G v2 - Cross-Trade Expansion (utilities 105 through 113) in calc-cross.js. Loan Payment uses payment = P*r / (1 - (1+r)^-n) with first 12 amortization rows. Upgrade ROI / Payback returns simple payback and 10-year NPV at user discount rate. Mileage and Fuel Cost computes gallons, fuel cost, and IRS reimbursement (rate from data/crosswalks/irs-mileage.json). Overtime applies 40 hr regular, 1.5x to a configurable double-time threshold, and 2.0x beyond. Per-Diem looks up GSA-published lodging or M&IE by state from data/crosswalks/gsa-perdiem.json. Geometry Pack covers circle (circumference, area, sector), ellipse (Ramanujan perimeter), regular hexagon, polygon perimeter, and sphere. Dilution / Mixing Ratio splits final volume into concentrate and diluent. Slope from Digital Level converts between degrees, percent, and inches per foot. GPS Distance uses the haversine formula plus the standard initial-bearing formula (R = 3958.8 mi / 6371.0088 km). New shards data/crosswalks/irs-mileage.json and data/crosswalks/gsa-perdiem.json wired into scripts/build-data.mjs (46 expected hashes). docs/data-sources.md, scripts/sources.md, and docs/derivations.md (section 24, haversine + bearing) updated. TOOL_DATA_SOURCES wired for mileage-cost and per-diem. New test/unit/calc-cross-v2.test.js with 90 cases; 747 unit tests passing. Lint and data:verify green.

- Step 28 complete (spec-v2.md): Group F v2 - Fire-Ground Engineering Expansion (utilities 100 through 104) in calc-fire.js. Reverse-Lay Supply Friction Loss extends the NFA CQ^2L formula to a tandem-pump scenario where the parallel section's per-pump friction scales as (1/n_pumps)^2. Sprinkler GPM Density returns total_gpm = area * density, with NFPA 13 hazard categories referenced by name only and a meets-minimum check. Standpipe Friction Loss sums riser elevation (0.434 psi/ft) plus per-outlet CQ^2L. Ladder Pipe Reach combines the existing aerial-ladder geometry with master-stream forward reach (cos 30 deg). Vehicle Braking Distance uses d = v^2 / (30 * (mu +/- grade%/100)) plus reaction distance v*1.467*t. docs/derivations.md (sections 22 tandem-pump, 23 braking) updated. New test/unit/calc-fire-v2.test.js with 50 cases; 657 unit tests passing at this step (cumulative 747 after Step 29). Lint and data:verify green.

- Step 27 complete (spec-v2.md): Group E v2 - Carpentry and Construction Expansion (utilities 90 through 99) in calc-construction.js. Stair Stringer Length uses Pythagorean over rise + run plus 2x12 board-foot estimate. Joist Mid-Span Deflection uses delta = 5 * w * L^4 / (384 * E * I) with L/360 and L/240 checks. Footing Area for Soil Bearing divides column load by allowable psf from the new soil-bearing.json shard, rounding side up to the next 6 in. Tile Count and Grout Volume sums waste-rounded tile count and grout cubic inches via joint perimeter * width * tile thickness. Paint Coverage uses 350/250/175 ft^2/gal benchmarks with porosity surface factors. Excavation Volume uses the frustum formula V = D/3 * (A1 + A2 + sqrt(A1*A2)) with set-back per side from depth and slope angle. Brick / CMU Count uses face-area waste-rounded count with mortar joint inflation. Wind Velocity Pressure applies the public ASCE 7 form q = 0.00256 * V^2 with windward (+0.8) and leeward (-0.5) Cp. Flat-Roof Snow Load applies Pf = 0.7 * Ce * Ct * Is * Pg. Anchor Bolt Embedment solves ld = T / (0.7 * sqrt(fc) * pi * d). New shards data/construction/soil-bearing.json and data/construction/wind-snow-zones.json wired into scripts/build-data.mjs (44 expected hashes). docs/data-sources.md, scripts/sources.md, and docs/derivations.md (sections 17 deflection, 18 excavation frustum, 19 wind, 20 snow, 21 anchor embedment) updated. TOOL_DATA_SOURCES wired for footing-area, wind-pressure, and snow-load. New test/unit/calc-construction-v2.test.js with 100 cases; 607 unit tests passing. Lint and data:verify green.

- Step 26 complete (spec-v2.md): Group D v2 - Restoration Expansion (utilities 86 through 89) in calc-restoration.js. Standing Water Volume uses gallons = area_ft^2 * depth_in / 12 * 7.48052 with weight at 62.4 lb/ft^3. Negative Air Machine Sizing uses required_CFM = volume * ACH / 60 and recommends unit counts at 500 / 1000 / 2000 CFM. HEPA Scrubber Filter Life Estimator uses filter_days = capacity_grams / (CFM * hours_per_day * loading_rate) with low/medium/high category rates. Thermal Imager Delta-T Reference is an original plain-English summary of typical surface-temperature differentials (NFA / OSHA training generally). New shard data/restoration/hepa-loading.json wired into scripts/build-data.mjs (42 expected hashes). docs/data-sources.md and scripts/sources.md updated. TOOL_DATA_SOURCES wired for thermal-delta-t. New test/unit/calc-restoration-v2.test.js with 37 cases; 507 unit tests passing. Lint and data:verify green.

- Step 25 complete (spec-v2.md): Group C v2 - HVAC Expansion (utilities 79 through 85) in calc-hvac.js. Refrigerant Charge Weighing sums oz per ft per line diameter per refrigerant from the new charge-per-foot.json shard. Approach and Delta-T Diagnostics computes condenser approach (T_sat - T_outdoor) and supply/return delta-T with low/normal/high banding. Outdoor Air Mix mass-mixes humidity ratios via the existing psychrometric helpers and weighted dry-bulb. Equivalent Length of Fittings sums the new equivalent-lengths.json table by fitting type and diameter. Wet-Bulb Sling Psychrometer solves the standard psychrometric wet-bulb relation for RH, dew point, and GPP. Pipe Insulation Thickness bisects r2 on Q = 2*pi*k*L*dT / ln(r2/r1) against an outside-film flux. Latent Heat Evaporative Cooling uses Q = m_dot * h_fg with h_fg ~ 1054 BTU/lb. New shards data/hvac/charge-per-foot.json, data/hvac/equivalent-lengths.json, and data/hvac/insulation.json wired into scripts/build-data.mjs (41 expected hashes). docs/data-sources.md, scripts/sources.md, and docs/derivations.md (sections 15 OA mixing and 16 cylindrical conduction) updated. TOOL_DATA_SOURCES wired for refrigerant-charge, equivalent-length, and insulation-thickness. New test/unit/calc-hvac-v2.test.js with 70 cases; 470 unit tests passing. Lint and data:verify green.

- Step 24 complete (spec-v2.md): Group B v2 - Plumbing and Gas Expansion (utilities 72 through 78) in calc-plumbing.js. Water Hammer Arrestor designation by PDI WH-201 method (six designations AA-A through AA-F). Hot Water Recirculation Pump Head reuses Hazen-Williams over the supply loop plus an equivalent-length allowance for fittings. Septic Tank Sizing applies 150 gpd per bedroom (or explicit gpd) with a 1000 gallon floor and the 2x daily-flow rule. Trap Arm Length combines a per-diameter table with a fall-limit (one pipe diameter total fall). Pipe Thermal Expansion uses dL (in) = alpha (1/F) * L (ft) * 12 * dT (F) with NIST / manufacturer-bulletin coefficients. Tankless Water Heater GPM uses gpm = kBTU * 1000 / (8.33 * 60 * dT) with NOAA inlet temperatures by climate zone. Gas Leak Rate uses Q = 3550 * c * A * sqrt(dP / SG). New shards data/plumbing/material-expansion.json and data/plumbing/septic-rules.json wired into scripts/build-data.mjs (38 expected hashes). docs/data-sources.md, scripts/sources.md, and docs/derivations.md (section 14, pipe thermal expansion) updated. TOOL_DATA_SOURCES wired for water-hammer-arrestor, trap-arm, and gas-leak-rate. New test/unit/calc-plumbing-v2.test.js with 70 cases; 400 unit tests passing. Lint and data:verify green.

- Step 23 complete (spec-v2.md): Group A v2 - Electrical Expansion (utilities 65 through 71) in calc-electrical.js. Service Load Calculation (Residential) sums general lighting (3 W/ft^2), small-appliance (2 x 1500 W default), laundry (1500 W), fixed appliances, range (first 8 kW at 100% then 40%), dryer (5 kW minimum), and HVAC (larger of cool vs heat); applies the standard residential demand factor (first 3000 W at 100% then 35%) and outputs required ampacity at 240 V plus the next standard service from [60, 100, 125, 150, 175, 200, 225, 250, 300, 400]. Generator Sizing returns continuous and surge wattage (surge = continuous + the largest motor's starting-running excess). Solar PV String Sizing computes cold-Voc max-series and warm-Vmp min-series for the inverter's MPPT and Vdc-max window with an infeasibility flag. Battery Runtime computes hours from Ah * V * DoD / load with Peukert form t = C / I^k when k > 1. Voltage Imbalance returns percent imbalance and the NEMA-form motor derate factor (1 - 2 * (imbalance/100)^2). GFCI/AFCI Requirements Reference and Lighting Power Density use plain-English benchmarks; NEC and ASHRAE 90.1 are referenced by section/name only. New data shards data/electrical/demand-factors.json, data/electrical/lighting-density.json, and data/summaries/v2-references.json wired into scripts/build-data.mjs and integrity (36 expected hashes; 9 manifests). docs/data-sources.md and scripts/sources.md updated. TOOL_DATA_SOURCES wired for gfci-afci-reference and lighting-density. New test/unit/calc-electrical-v2.test.js with 68 cases across the seven utilities; 330 unit tests passing. Lint and data:verify green.

### Polish

- Static HTML changelog view at changelog.html with same-origin styling, fetched and rendered as plain text by changelog.js (no innerHTML, no Markdown library); replaces the raw CHANGELOG.md link in the footer per spec section 14 step 20.
- scripts/derivations.md added per spec section 6 file layout; the authoritative record remains in docs/derivations.md.
- Brand mark added: favicon.svg is a monochrome 18-tooth gear that matches the user-supplied logo.jpg (brand source kept in the repo root, not shipped to dist). icon and apple-touch-icon link tags reference the same SVG so the runtime payload stays minimal. site.webmanifest icons array updated.
- Hash state wired per spec section 11.5. New hash-state.js exposes applyHashState (populate inputs/selects/checkboxes from URL params on tool open) and wireHashState (write current input state back to the URL hash via history.replaceState, debounced 100 ms). app.js renderToolView calls both for every calculator so calculator state is bookmarkable and shareable without localStorage. Pin / Unpin buttons added to every tile (toggling state.pinned and re-rendering with aria-pressed) and a "Pin to home / Unpin from home" button added to each tool view header. styles.css gains tile-actions, tile-pin, view-header-row, and view-pin styles preserving 48 px touch targets and the monochrome palette. Five new hash-state unit tests, 225 total passing.
- Pinned section rendered at the top of the home view (id="pinned-region") with a "Clear pins" affordance. Visible only when state.pinned is non-empty. Pin/unpin from a home tile or via the home-route applyRoute now writes the hash to #p=... per spec section 11.5; navigating to a #p=... bookmark restores the pinned set. Pinning from a tool view updates in-memory state; the URL is rewritten with #p=... the next time the home route is rendered. styles.css adds .pinned-header and .pinned-title.
- Per spec section 11.7, every reference-style utility now displays a "Source: <dataset>, version <X>, fetched <Y>." line on its view. New data-stamp.js exposes fetchManifest (cached), stampDataSource (appends a per-view source line from the relevant data/<folder>/manifest.json), and stampFooterVersion (replaces the "Data version: pending" footer text with the build timestamp from build-info.json or the physical-constants manifest version). app.js carries a TOOL_DATA_SOURCES table mapping 21 reference-style tool ids to their manifest folder/shard/label; renderToolView calls stampDataSource for matching ids. First-principles calculators continue to cite physics inline only. New .sources-region and .data-source-stamp styles in styles.css.
- Runtime data-integrity check per spec section 7. scripts/build-data.mjs now emits data/integrity.json containing the SHA-256 hash of each per-folder manifest. New integrity.js fetches that sidecar at boot and verifies every manifest via SubtleCrypto SHA-256. A mismatch (or missing/unfetchable manifest) emits a console error and inserts a non-blocking banner above the main content naming the affected dataset(s). Skips gracefully when SubtleCrypto is unavailable (e.g., http://example, dev fallback). 4 new unit tests using a fetch + DOM stub and Node's webcrypto, 229 total passing. docs/threat-model.md updated to reflect the implementation.
- N-gram code-text duplicate detector per spec section 13. New scripts/check-ngrams.mjs walks project text files (md/html/css/js/mjs/json/txt), tokenizes Unicode-letter+digit runs, and SHA-256-hashes every 25-token span (configurable via NGRAM_SIZE), comparing against a private fingerprint list at scripts/banned-ngrams.json (gitignored). Skips gracefully when the list is absent (the public-repo default), so the public CI run is non-blocking; environments with the list mounted at the expected path (or NGRAM_LIST env var) run the full scan and fail the build on any verbatim or near-verbatim 25-word match against NEC/IPC/IRC/IECC/IFC/IBC/ASHRAE/ACCA/NFPA/AWC published text. scripts/banned-ngrams.example.json documents the policy; npm run lint chains grep-checks and check-ngrams. Detector verified end-to-end against a planted 25-token fixture.
- Home-view payload trimmed under the spec section 11.1 100 KB budget. app.js now imports calculator modules (calc-electrical/plumbing/hvac/restoration/construction/fire/cross.js) and their support libs (hash-state.js, data-stamp.js, and transitively pure-math.js) via dynamic import() inside renderToolView; each module is fetched once on first tool open and cached by both the in-memory promise cache and the service worker. The footer-version stamp is deferred to requestIdleCallback so it does not delay FCP. Home-view files now total about 52 KB uncompressed (index.html + styles.css + app.js + integrity.js); calculator views load their module + support libs on demand. docs/performance.md updated to reflect the lazy-loading strategy. 229 unit tests still passing.
- Copy-all and live-region announcer per spec section 11.3. New clipboard.js exports copyText (Clipboard API + "Copied" announcement), addCopyAllButton (visible only when the output region has 2+ labeled rows; emits a labeled multi-line plaintext summary prefixed with the tool name), collectOutputs (label/value pair extraction from the output DOM), and announce. renderToolView wires addCopyAllButton generically so the affordance applies to all 64 utilities without per-calculator changes. A MutationObserver re-evaluates Copy-all visibility when the output region updates (e.g., when an example button populates or when the live result count changes). 4 new clipboard unit tests using a DOM stub, 233 total passing.
- Invalid-input behavior per spec section 11.2. New ui-validity.js delegates validity to HTML5 checkValidity() so existing min/max/step/required/pattern attributes drive the experience. On invalid: aria-invalid is set on the input, a brief plain-text reason (the browser's validationMessage) is rendered next to the field via a .validity-reason span, and the output region gains an .output-stale class that strikes through every output value via styles.css. Cleared once every input is valid again. wireValidity is loaded with the support libs and called from renderToolView, applying generically to all 64 utilities without per-calculator changes. 4 new ui-validity unit tests using a DOM stub with checkValidity stubs, 237 total passing.
- data-stamp.js test coverage. 8 new tests using fetch + DOM stubs verifying fetchManifest caches by folder and returns null on failure (no cache poisoning), stampDataSource emits the exact "Source: <label>, version <X>, fetched <Y>." format from the manifest, falls back to the manifest's per-shard `name` when no caller label is supplied, gracefully reports "manifest unavailable" when the fetch fails, and stampFooterVersion prefers build-info.json's timestamp, falls back to the physical-constants manifest version, and writes "Data version: dev" when nothing is available. 245 total passing.
- Routing helpers extracted to routing.js (parseHashRoute, decodePinnedList, toolMatches) so they can be unit-tested without a DOM stub. app.js delegates parseHash and matchesFilters to the pure helpers, eliminating duplication. 17 new routing unit tests covering the spec section 11.5 hash format invariants: empty/home/known/unknown tool ids, calculator state params, pinned format with whitespace and unknown-id filtering, defaulting on bad input; trade and group filter matching including multi-trade tools; case-insensitive query search across name and description. 262 total passing.
- Form-field helpers centralized into ui-fields.js (DEBOUNCE_MS, debounce, makeNumber, makeText, makeSelect, makeCheckbox, makeOutputLine, attachExampleButton, fmt). All seven calc-*.js modules removed their local copies and import from the shared module; the per-output Copy button now goes through clipboard.copyText so every Copy emits the "Copied" announcement consistently. 44 duplicate helper definitions deleted; calc bundle dropped from ~199 KB to ~182 KB plus a single 3.7 KB ui-fields.js shared on first calc-view load. 262 unit tests still passing; lint clean.

## v0.8.0 - 2026-05-07

The v8 audit, citation-polish, and field-reality refinement pass. No new groups, no new licenses, no new third-party dependencies, no new storage keys, no new state mechanism. The May 2026 deep correctness audit found no critical math or logic bugs across 206 exported compute functions; v8 closes the last ten percent that separates a correct tool from a tool a tradesperson reaches for first - smart defaults, companion outputs, round-to-next-standard-part, context bands, costs added to quantity tools, and the v6 citation discipline applied tile-by-tile to the code-derived utilities. Adds five new utilities (254-258) for an obvious-gap close.

Highlights:

- **Phase A - data manifest discipline.** Every `data/*/manifest.json` shard now declares an `edition` field (for code-locked data) or an `asOf` field (for date-stamped data) per spec-v6 §7. New `scripts/check-manifests.mjs` lint fails CI if any manifest is missing either field; chained into `npm run lint`. asOf added to all 11 manifests; edition stamps confirmed on every code-derived shard.

- **Phase B - citation discipline applied tile-by-tile.** ~25 source-stamp strings polished across calc-electrical / calc-plumbing / calc-hvac / calc-fire / calc-construction / calc-kitchen / calc-trucking / calc-mechanic to include code edition, section number, AHJ-governs notice, and free-access URL. wire-ampacity / conduit-fill / box-fill / service-load / breaker-sizing / motor-fla / egc / lighting-density / gfci-afci-reference cite NEC 2023 by section. pipe-sizing / gas-pipe-sizing / friction-loss / vent-sizing / septic-tank / grease-trap cite IPC 2021, IFGC 2021, EPA Onsite Wastewater Manual. duct-sizing / refrigerant-pt / combustion-air cite IMC 2021 / ASHRAE 15-2022. sprinkler-density / required-fire-flow / pdp / standpipe-friction cite NFPA 13-2022 / IFC 2021 / NFPA 14-2022. lumber-spans / rafter / stair / footing-area cite IRC 2021 / IBC 2021 / AWC NDS-2018. cook-temps / hos-math / bridge-formula / weight-balance cite FDA Food Code 2022 / FMCSA 49 CFR 395 / 23 CFR 658.17 / FAA AC 91-23A.

- **Phase C - 29 tile renderers wired** across four batches (batch 1: 6, batch 2: 8, batch 3: 8, batch 4: 7). Every Phase C compute field now has a renderer surface. Highlights by group: transformer-sizing ANSI/IEEE C57 step badge; voltage-drop voltage-at-load + status; voltage-imbalance NEMA MG-1 HP derate; conduit-fill PASS / FAIL badge + margin; breaker-sizing watts + voltage + phase + pf input mode. friction-loss velocity + status; gas-pipe-sizing achieved dP; expansion-tank pre-charge + placement; water-hammer-arrestor pre-charge. manual-j-heating tons row; superheat-subcool diagnostic band; cfm-per-ton climate hint; duct-sizing friction-rate band; refrigerant-pt target superheat. concrete 60/80 lb bag count; lumber-spans deflection inches; asphalt-tonnage paving distance + per-truck rows. dim-weight billing-basis + break-even cube; pallet-loadout binding margin + slack utilization; reefer-burn fuel reserve at end of haul; hos-math next legal drive start as ISO timestamp. fuel-range cost-per-mile; brake-pad-life cost-per-100k mi; weight-balance %MAC; displacement-cr premium-octane flag. dehumidifier operational guidance; air-mover placement pattern + note; hepa-filter-life full-job filter count + total cost; timber-cruise stand-value.

- **Phase D - three shared helpers.** `cost-output.js` (`formatCostOutput(quantity, unitPrice, unitName)` for quantity-output tiles; price never persisted). `context-band.js` (`formatContextBand(value, low, high, unit)` for low / normal / high beside Manual J / CFM-per-ton / superheat / subcool / approach / voltage-drop / pipe-velocity / cooling-tower flow). `standard-sizes.js` (`roundToStandard(value, standardSizes)` ladders for transformer kVA / breaker amps / pump HP / water heater gal / service amps; returns recommended + at_floor + at_cap).

- **Phase E - five new utilities (254-258).** `panel-rebalance` (utility 254, calc-electrical.js): per-circuit row list with phase A/B/C placement + a swap-list optimization to minimize imbalance under existing breaker-position constraints; cites NEC 2023 §220 by name. `trap-arm` (utility from v2; v8 confirms IPC 2021 §909 + Table 909.1 citation). `duct-leakage` (utility 255, calc-hvac.js): SMACNA Duct Leakage Test Manual classes + design-CFM / measured-CFM pass / fail with optional cost-of-lost-efficiency. `residential-framing` (utility 256, calc-construction.js): footprint sq ft / wall height / roof pitch / joist span / rafter span -> stud counts (16" + 24" o.c.), top + bottom plate board feet, joist + rafter counts + total board feet, ridge board, one-line lumber order summary; cites IRC 2021 R502.5 / R602.5 / R802.5.1. `coagulant-dose` (utility 257, calc-water.js): jar-test optimal dose -> lb/day + gal/day at standard liquid stock strengths (alum 48.5%, ferric 12.5% Fe) + chemical cost; cites Metcalf & Eddy + AWWA M37 by name.

- **Test coverage.** 491 new unit tests across calc-historical (25), citations (66), v7 expansions (170), v8 phases A-E (98), and 29 renderer-wiring tests across four v8-renderer-wiring batches. 2293 unit tests passing total; lint clean (edition stamps + free-access doc coverage + citation-string advisory + manifest-discipline + home-payload); integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.4% of 100 KB budget; build 143 files / 1533.4 KB. Lighthouse / accessibility / performance gates from prior releases unaffected.

### Pre-release build progress (rolled into v0.8.0)

- v8 §C.1 wire-ampacity ambient preset chips landed. The exported `WIRE_AMPACITY_AMBIENT_PRESETS` table (Indoor 30 C / Field 45 C / Extreme 60 C) is now wired through `renderWireAmpacity` as a horizontal `<button class="preset-chip">` group below the ambient input, wrapped in `<div role="group" aria-label="Ambient temperature presets">`. Each chip prefills the ambient field and re-runs compute. New `.preset-chip-row` + `.preset-chip` styles in [styles.css](styles.css) carry `min-height: var(--touch-min)` (48 px platform default; 64 px in Big Buttons mode via the existing global override). Cuts the common case from four taps to one per spec-v8.md §C.1.

- v8 §D.2 `formatContextBand` shared helper wired into its first two renderer surfaces. `manual-j-cooling` ([calc-hvac.js](calc-hvac.js)) gains a "BTU/hr per sq ft (typical 15-30)" row that classifies the load as low / normal / high against the residential cooling band; `manual-j-heating` gains the same row at 25-50 BTU/hr per sq ft. The helper itself was authored in Phase D but had no renderer surface; this is the first user-visible application. The band only renders when floor_area_ft2 and total_BTU_hr are both positive (no spurious "low" classification on an empty form). 3 new regression tests in [test/unit/v8-context-band-wiring.test.js](test/unit/v8-context-band-wiring.test.js).

- v8 preset-chip pattern extended to three more tiles. New shared `COMMON_VOLTAGE_PRESETS` table in [calc-electrical.js](calc-electrical.js) (120 / 208 / 240 / 277 / 480 V) is wired into both `voltage-drop` (source voltage) and `breaker-sizing` (watts-input voltage). New `REFRIGERANT_OAT_PRESETS` table in [calc-hvac.js](calc-hvac.js) (Mild 75 / Design 85 / Hot 95 / Extreme 105 F; aligned with AHRI 210/240 + ASHRAE design conditions) is wired into `refrigerant-pt` so the field tech sets the OAT for the target-superheat lookup with one tap. All three rows reuse the existing `.preset-chip-row` CSS and `<button class="preset-chip">` + `role="group"` markup. 5 new regression tests in [test/unit/v8-preset-chips-batch3.test.js](test/unit/v8-preset-chips-batch3.test.js).

- v8 preset-chip pattern extended to two more tiles. `duct-sizing` ([calc-hvac.js](calc-hvac.js)) gains a friction-rate chip row (Low 0.06 / Typical 0.08 / High 0.10) keyed to ACCA Manual D bands; the new `DUCT_FRICTION_PRESETS` table is exported so future renderer tests can pin the values. `water-hammer-arrestor` ([calc-plumbing.js](calc-plumbing.js)) gains a system-pressure chip row (Low 40 psi / Typical 60 psi / High 80 psi) so the tech can pre-fill the optional system-pressure input with one tap and let the compute return the matching arrestor pre-charge value. Both rows reuse the `<button class="preset-chip">` + `role="group"` markup and the `.preset-chip-row` CSS introduced in the prior batch; no new CSS, no new state mechanism. 4 new regression tests in [test/unit/v8-preset-chips-batch2.test.js](test/unit/v8-preset-chips-batch2.test.js).

- v8 §9.4 doc deliverables landed. New [docs/citation-discipline.md](docs/citation-discipline.md) is the single source of truth for the user-visible source-stamp strings (Phase B output) so future edition rolls (NEC 2026, IPC 2024, IRC 2024, ASHRAE 62.1-2025, FDA Food Code 2026) update one file and propagate. Includes per-source free-access URL table and per-tile source-stamp strings for Groups A, B, C, E, F, J, K, O. [docs/accessibility.md](docs/accessibility.md) gains a "v8 preset chips" section documenting the `<button class="preset-chip">` + `role="group"` pattern, the touch-min contract, the dark / light / high-contrast theme flow, and the deliberate scope (chips prefill numeric fields and re-run compute; they are not toggles or radio buttons).

- 5 new regression tests in [test/unit/v8-preset-chips.test.js](test/unit/v8-preset-chips.test.js) assert the chip-row markup, the preset table contents, the .preset-chip touch-min style, and the doc deliverables. 2298 unit tests passing total; lint clean; home-view payload 40.6% of 100 KB; build 143 files / 1543.5 KB.

## v0.7.0 - 2026-05-07

The v7 expansion. Twenty new utilities (234 through 253) across six groups, plus thirteen new data shards. Tool count grows from two hundred thirty-three to two hundred fifty-three spec-numbered utilities; visible-tile count grows from 221 to 241.

Highlights:

- **Group A v7 - Electrical (utilities 234-237).** transformer-kva-sizing (ANSI/IEEE C57 step series + FLA), short-circuit-pp (Bussmann point-to-point method with C-values shard), generator-motor-starting (NEMA MG-1 code-letter table at the 30% voltage-dip criterion), service-load-standard (NEC 2023 Article 220 Standard Method demand-factor walk).

- **Group B v7 - Plumbing and Hydronics (utilities 238-241).** water-hammer-surge (Joukowsky a = sqrt(K/rho) / sqrt(1 + (K D)/(E t)); 6 pipe materials + 3 fluids + 8 Schedule-40 sizes), pump-operating-point (binary-search intersection with bundled curves; pure-DOM SVG plot), septic-drainfield (deliberately unbundled per-state shard; AHJ-supplied application rate), pipe-expansion-loop (ASME B31.1 / B31.9 guided-cantilever loop leg).

- **Group C v7 - HVAC (utilities 242-245).** duct-friction-static (Darcy-Weisbach with Swamee-Jain Colebrook; Huebscher equivalent diameter), refrigerant-charging (P-T tables for 5 refrigerants with per-input psig / psia toggle), cooling-tower (range / approach / heat rejection / fan kW per ton), insulation-heat-loss (cylindrical conduction + convection + radiation with iterative outer-surface T solve).

- **Group E v7 - Carpentry and Construction (utilities 246-251).** stair-stringer-layout (with AHJ-supplied code-check), hip-valley-rafter (framing-square method with irregular-hip second pitch), rebar-schedule (ASTM A615 + CRSI bend allowances), plywood-span (APA span-rating tables), helical-pile (ICC-ES AC358 + manufacturer Kt), crane-lift-quick (refuses output without user-entered chart capacity; ASME B30.5 governs).

- **Group F v7 - Fire-Ground (utility 252).** iso-nff (ISO Public Protection Classification NFF formula with stories cap, exposure-distance bands, 250 gpm rounding, 12 000 gpm cap).

- **Group G v7 - Cross-Trade (utility 253).** fall-protection-clearance (29 CFR 1926.502 + ANSI Z359; manufacturer connector-decel benchmarks).

- **Thirteen new data shards.** data/electrical/conductor-c-values.json + nema-mg1-code-letters.json + dwelling-demand.json (v7 §A); data/plumbing/pipe-elastic-properties.json + pump-curves.json + thermal-expansion-coefficients.json (v7 §B); data/hvac/duct-roughness.json + duct-fittings.json + refrigerant-pt-tables.json + insulation-k-values.json (v7 §C); data/construction/rebar-unit-weights.json + apa-span-ratings.json + helical-pile-kt.json (v7 §E); data/fire/iso-nff.json (v7 §F); data/crosswalks/fall-protection-benchmarks.json (v7 §G).

- **Two new GOVERNANCE variants** in citations.js: engineer_of_record (rebar-schedule, helical-pile, crane-lift-quick, fall-protection-clearance) and worker_safety. Every v7 tile has a structured §3 reference block; the v6-completion coverage test (every tile id in app.js has a CITATIONS entry) continues to pass.

- **docs/derivations.md** gained eighteen new sections (30-47) covering every v7 utility's first-principles math. **docs/data-sources.md** + **scripts/sources.md** gained one entry per new shard.

- **Test coverage.** 222 new unit tests across calc-electrical-v7 (40), calc-plumbing-v7 (33), calc-hvac-v7 (39), calc-construction-v7 (46), calc-fire-v7 (12), calc-cross-v7 (12), and citations.test.js v7-completion updates. 2075 unit tests passing total; lint clean (edition stamps + free-access doc coverage); integrity 96 entries / 11 datasets; home-view payload 40.0% of 100 KB budget; build 140 files / 1425 KB. Lighthouse / accessibility / performance gates from prior releases unaffected.

## v0.6.0 - 2026-05-07

The v6 citation-discipline pass. No new utilities; the deliverable is the discipline. Every visible tile in the catalog (221 tiles across sixteen groups A-H plus J-Q) now carries a structured §3 reference block: formula or table cited, edition / source date, public free-access pointer, governance notice from spec §2.5 (one of fifteen variants), edition selector / disclosure, and a numeric-assumptions list source-stamped per row. The "Copy answer with full reference block" button writes the same block as a plain-text snippet a tradesperson can paste into a job log, RFI, permit application, or text to the foreman.

Highlights:

- **Every tile cites by section and edition.** Not "per NEC." Per NEC 310.16 (2023) with a 75 °C termination column, 30 °C ambient, and ≤ 3 CCC default. Per IPC 2021 §709 fixture units. Per ASCE 7-22 §26.10 (q = 0.00256 V² Kz Kzt Kd Ke). Per IFGC 2021 §304.5 (1 sq in / 1000 BTU/hr). Per FDA Food Code 2022 §3-501.14 (135-70-41 °F cooling curve). Per FMCSA 49 CFR 395.3 (11 / 14 / 70-8 / 60-7). Per 23 CFR 658.17 (W = 500 (LN/(N-1) + 12N + 36)). Per ICC Incoterms 2020 (eleven rules by name). Per IICRC S500-2021 §10 / S520-2024 §12. Per EPA SWTR 40 CFR 141. Per AWS Welding Handbook (SMAW 65% / GMAW 92% deposition efficiencies). Per FAA AC 91-23A. Per ABYC P-17. Per NIOSH 1991 (load constant 51 lb). Per USGS PP 1395 (Snyder Krueger). Per NOAA SPA (Reda-Andreas, NREL/TP-560-34302). Plus AHJ-disclosure on every code-derived tile and "edition note" disclosing where bundled values differ from older editions.

- **Free-access pointer named on every tile.** "Free read-only access at nfpa.org/freeaccess." "Free at codes.iccsafe.org." "Free at ecfr.gov." "Free at fdc.nal.usda.gov." "Free at hdsc.nws.noaa.gov." "Free at usfa.fema.gov." Plus first-party citations to free engineering pubs (ARMA, NCMA TEK, BIA Tech Notes, GA-216, USDA NRCS NEH, AIARE, USFS NAC, USGS, NIST SP 811, NOAA WMM, USDA FoodData Central). The user copies the name and goes to look it up themselves; no outbound links at runtime.

- **Governance notice sized to the stakes** (spec §2.5). Fifteen variants in `citations.js` GOVERNANCE map: general, electrical, plumbing, structural, mechanical, fire, pesticide ("The label is the law (FIFRA)"), trucking ("The ELD on the truck and the carrier tariff are the legal record"), aviation ("Pilot-in-command and the airplane flight manual govern"), marine ("Vessel master governs"), food ("The thermometer on the food is the verdict"), water ("Operator of record and primacy agency govern"), rigging ("Head rigger and manufacturer working-load-limit charts govern"), field ("Geometry is not forecasting"), reference. Every tile uses the spec wording verbatim; tests enforce verbatim per group.

- **Numeric assumptions list** beneath every reference block. The point is that an inspector or senior tradesperson can reproduce the answer without re-deriving the constants. Examples: voltage-drop discloses 75 °C termination + 30 °C ambient + 3% branch / 5% feeder target. Conduit-fill discloses NEC Chapter 9 Table 5 THHN/THWN-2 areas + Table 4 trade sizes. Footing-area discloses the IBC 2021 Table 1806.2 bearing-capacity table by soil class. NPSHa discloses ICAO Standard Atmosphere lapse + 2.31 ft H2O / psi conversion. Cooling-curve discloses TCS-food assumption per FDA Food Code §1-201.10. Bridge-formula discloses 20k single / 34k tandem / 80k Interstate caps. Driveshaft-crit discloses steel E = 30e6 psi / ρ = 0.283 lb/in³ default + 0.65 × N_crit operating margin per AAM/Spicer.

- **Build-pipeline foundation.** `scripts/build-data.mjs` carries an `edition` field per dataset (NIST CODATA 2018 / NEC 2023 / IPC 2021 / IFGC 2021 / ASHRAE 62.1-2022 / ACCA Manual J 8th / IICRC S500-2021 + S520-2024 / IRC 2021 / IBC 2021 / ASCE 7-22 / AWC NDS-2018 / FMCSA 49 CFR 395 / 23 CFR 658.17 / NFA / ISO PPC / NIST SP 811 / IRS 2024 mileage / GSA FY2026 / NIOSH 1991 / OSHA 29 CFR 1926 / BLS PPI / EIA / USDA NASS / FRED). Build-time prose-lint flags string values longer than 140 characters that look like prose paste-ins. `scripts/check-v6-discipline.mjs` adds free-access lint cross-referencing every shipped shard against `docs/data-sources.md` (with wildcard support for fan-out shards) and an advisory citation-string lint counting inline `"per <Source>"` strings in `calc-*.js`. All three lints chained into `npm run lint` so a CI failure blocks deploys.

- **Audit tracker.** `docs/v6-audit.md` records the per-tile checklist + priority-ordered group list + the 2026-05-07 audit-completion close-out. Coverage test in `test/unit/citations.test.js` parses every tile id from `app.js` and asserts a `CITATIONS` entry exists; the build fails if a future tile is added without one.

- **UI integration.** `app.js` dynamically imports `citations.js` on every tool view, mounts the §3 reference block under the existing `sources-region` (CSS picks up dark / light / high-contrast theme + Big Buttons mode automatically), and appends the "Copy answer with full reference block" button. Tiles not covered by `CITATIONS` fall through to the legacy inline citation; the audit close-out means every tile in the catalog now ships the structured block.

- **Test coverage.** 1893 unit tests passing total (66 in `test/unit/citations.test.js`); lint clean; integrity 81 entries across 11 datasets; build 125 files / 1244 KB; home-view payload 37.6% of the 100 KB budget. Lighthouse / accessibility / performance gates from prior releases unaffected (the reference block is a static `<dl>`, no new behavior or third-party dependency).

## v0.4.0 - 2026-05-07

The v4 expansion (the "Stay Dirty Pack"). Tool count grows from one hundred seventy-five visible tiles to two hundred twenty-one (or "two hundred thirty-three utilities" by spec numbering, since several v3 utilities ship as platform affordances rather than tiles), organized across sixteen category sections (the original eight trades plus v4 Groups J - Q): Trucking and Logistics, Mechanic / Auto / Marine / Aviation, Agriculture and Forestry, Water and Wastewater Operations, Stage and Live Production, Kitchen and Food Service, Field / Backcountry / SAR, and the new Group Q: Historical Reference Data. 1827 unit tests passing across v1 + v2 + v3 + v4, lint clean, data:verify clean (81 entries / 11 datasets), home-view payload 37.0% of the 100 KB budget after every new tool registration, every new calc module dynamic-imports on first use, and every new dataset is bundled under data/.

Highlights:

- Group J Trucking and Logistics (188 - 194): DIM weight, freight density / NMFTA class, pallet load-out, FMCSA Hours-of-Service, Federal Bridge Formula, reefer fuel burn, Incoterms 2020 decoder.
- Group K Mechanic, Auto / Marine / Aviation (195 - 202): aircraft weight-and-balance, propeller slip, displacement and compression ratio, bolt stretch, driveshaft critical RPM, fuel range, tire / gearing, brake-pad life.
- Group L Agriculture and Forestry (203 - 209): GPA / sprayer rate, timber cruise (Doyle / Scribner / International 1/4), seed rate, drawbar power, irrigation uniformity, bulk density, crop yield.
- Group M Water and Wastewater Operations (210 - 215): pounds formula, filter loading, detention time, lab dilution / serial dilution, pump wire-to-water efficiency, SRT / F-to-M ratio.
- Group N Stage and Live Production (216 - 221): truss capacity, time alignment, DMX universe planner, neutral-conductor imbalance, SPL with distance, rigging WLL with sling angle.
- Group O Kitchen and Food Service (222 - 226): recipe scaling, yield-EP percentage, FDA cooling curve, plate cost / menu pricing, steam-table / pan conversion.
- Group P Field, Backcountry, and SAR (227 - 232): pacing, magnetic / true bearing, slope and avalanche window, backcountry water and calorie demand, UTM / lat-lon round-trip, NOAA solar position.
- Group Q Historical Reference Data (233): bundled monthly history per commodity (BLS PPI / EIA / USDA NASS / FRED) with 25 / 50 / 75 / 90 percentile bands over a user-selected lookback. Reference only; no live fetch, no alerts, no subscriptions, no telemetry. Build fails if any shard's latest point is more than 30 days behind the build date.
- Two new data folders: `data/trucking/` (DIM divisors, reefer-burn benchmarks) and `data/historical/commodities/` (one shard per commodity, fourteen total, each carrying its federal series ID).
- Build-pipeline fix: `scripts/build.mjs` and `sw.js` now enumerate every v3 / v4 calc module so production deploys ship them as static assets (without this fix, lazy-imported v3 / v4 modules would 404 outside dev). `scripts/build-data.mjs` learned to create subfolder shard directories so `commodities/copper.json` writes correctly.
- Documentation: `docs/data-sources.md`, `docs/derivations.md` (new section 29 on percentile bands), `docs/legal.md`, and `scripts/sources.md` now describe every v4 shard, every new derivation, and the no-runtime-fetch / no-alerts posture for the historical pricing tool.

- Group F v3 (Fire-Ground, utilities 159-161): confined space air change, rope rescue MA, sling angle.
- Group G v3 (Cross-Trade, utilities 162-173): OSHA trench sloping, NIOSH lifting, heat stress, wind chill, ladder angle, pulley MA, ramp slope, rainwater yield, daily timesheet, vehicle load, plus two meta-utilities (Job Estimate Roll-Up and Material Order List) that compose existing session state.
- Group H v3 (References, utilities 174-179): hand signals, OSHA Top-10, lockout/tagout, defensible space, FEMA P-320 storm shelter, START triage with hardened "not medical advice" notice.
- Group I v3 (Platform): Job Pack (utility 180) - a printable job sheet over recents and bundled inputs; Big Buttons mode (utility 182) bumping every interactive element to 64 px; High-Contrast theme (utility 183) with WCAG AAA pure-black/pure-white pairings and a yellow focus ring; Field Notes scratchpad (utility 185) bound to the URL hash key `k=`; Crash-Safe Resume (utility 187) wrapping every renderer in a try/catch boundary that preserves the URL hash on failure.
- 17 new data shards in `data/electrical/`, `data/plumbing/`, `data/hvac/`, `data/construction/`, `data/crosswalks/`, and `data/summaries/`. All source values are public domain, manufacturer-attributed, or original creative work; no licensed code text is reproduced.
- 25 new derivation sections in docs/derivations.md covering capstan, PoE, PF correction, multi-load VD, rational method, Manning slope, expansion tank, hydrostatic test, affinity laws, V-belt length, air receiver, NPSHa, containment orifice flow, ACI 211 mix design, bolt torque, bend allowance, SFM-to-RPM, AWS deposition, ACI 347 formwork, capstan-and-pulley MA with friction, sling angle, NIOSH lifting, NWS heat index / wind chill, vehicle axle balance.
- Brand and UX polish: tab title trimmed to "Rough Logic" (the visible tagline now reads "tools for the trade."), section headers drop the "Group A / B / C" prefix in favor of just the category name, search bar gets native datalist autocomplete that routes straight to the matched tool.

Deferred to v3.x: utility 181 (QR of current URL - needs a bundled MIT QR library that has to be dynamic-imported to stay under the home-payload budget), utility 184 (numpad layout toggle - `inputmode="decimal"` already does the right thing), utility 186 (Send To Other Device - depends on utility 181). All three will land in a follow-on point release.

## v0.2.0 - 2026-05-05

The v2 expansion. Tool count grows from sixty-four to one hundred nineteen, plus six cross-cutting platform affordances. Every utility ships under the same v1 envelope: same-origin static assets, deterministic compute, no telemetry, no LLM, no third-party fetches at runtime, no licensed code text bundled. 802 unit tests passing across the v1 + v2 surface at the v0.2.0 cut (836 after subsequent unreleased polish), lint and data:verify green, 46 manifest hashes verified at boot.

Highlights:

- Group A v2 (utilities 65-71): Service Load Calculation (Residential), Generator Sizing, Solar PV String Sizing, Battery Runtime (with Peukert), Voltage Imbalance, GFCI/AFCI Reference, Lighting Power Density.
- Group B v2 (utilities 72-78): Water Hammer Arrestor (PDI WH-201), Hot Water Recirc Pump Head, Septic Tank Sizing, Trap Arm Length, Pipe Thermal Expansion, Tankless Water Heater GPM, Gas Leak Rate (orifice).
- Group C v2 (utilities 79-85): Refrigerant Charge Weighing, Approach and Delta-T Diagnostics, Outdoor Air Mix, Equivalent Length of Fittings, Wet-Bulb Sling Psychrometer, Pipe Insulation Thickness, Latent Heat Evaporative Cooling.
- Group D v2 (utilities 86-89): Standing Water Volume, NAM Sizing, HEPA Scrubber Filter Life, Thermal Imager Delta-T Reference.
- Group E v2 (utilities 90-99): Stair Stringer Length, Joist Mid-Span Deflection, Footing Area for Soil Bearing, Tile Count and Grout Volume, Paint Coverage, Excavation Volume, Brick / CMU Count, Wind Velocity Pressure, Snow Load (ASCE 7), Anchor Bolt Embedment.
- Group F v2 (utilities 100-104): Reverse-Lay Tandem-Pump Friction, Sprinkler GPM Density, Standpipe Friction Loss, Ladder Pipe Reach, Vehicle Braking Distance.
- Group G v2 (utilities 105-113): Loan Payment, Upgrade ROI / Payback, Mileage and Fuel Cost (IRS rate), Overtime Hours, Per-Diem (GSA), Geometry Pack, Dilution / Mixing Ratio, Slope from Digital Level, GPS Distance (haversine).
- Group H new (utilities 114-118): Wire / Pipe / Gas Color Codes, Knot Reference, Inspection Prep Checklist, Utility Locator and Emergency Contacts, Tool Maintenance Intervals.
- Group I cross-cutting (utilities 119-124): Compare Refrigerants (Group C side-by-side P-T view), Recent Tools, Project Bundle (URL + JSON), Print / PDF view, Offline status indicator, Example deep-link and Copy share link. All shipped.

Data: 13 new shards across electrical (demand-factors, lighting-density), plumbing (material-expansion, septic-rules), hvac (charge-per-foot, equivalent-lengths, insulation), restoration (hepa-loading), construction (soil-bearing, wind-snow-zones), crosswalks (irs-mileage, gsa-perdiem), summaries (v2-references). 46 manifest hashes verified at boot. Every shard cited in docs/data-sources.md and scripts/sources.md.

Derivations: 14 new sections in docs/derivations.md (PV string sizing, battery Peukert, pipe thermal expansion, OA mixing, cylindrical conduction, joist deflection, excavation frustum, wind velocity pressure, snow load, anchor bolt embedment, tandem-pump friction, vehicle braking, haversine + bearing).

Architecture: Home-view payload remains under the 100 KB budget. All v2 calc-*.js modules continue to be dynamic-imported on first tool open. New modules: calc-references.js (Group H), bundle.js (utility 121).

Operations: No A/B testing, no flags, no tracking, no email capture, no notifications. Same-origin Blob URLs for the Bundle Download action. CSP unchanged.

## v0.1.0 - 2026-05-04

Initial complete build of roughlogic.com per spec.md, sections 1 through 16. All 22 numbered build steps in spec section 14 implemented and verified locally. 220 unit tests passing across pure-math, all six trade groups, the cross-trade group, and the first-principles verification suite. Lint and grep checks green. Data integrity green across 33 manifest and shard hashes. Build produces 53 files / ~290 KB total in dist/. Ready for first deploy to Cloudflare Pages; the launch checklist in docs/launch-checklist.md enumerates the deploy-time gates that remain.

### Build progress

- Step 1 complete: repository scaffolding per spec.md section 6.
- Step 2 complete: documentation skeleton in docs/.
- Step 3 complete: README per spec.md section 14 step 3.
- Step 4 complete: visual skeleton in index.html and styles.css with CSP meta tag, header, search box, trade and group filters, tile grid, footer disclaimer.
- Step 5 complete: hash-based routing in app.js, tool registry of all 64 utilities, trade and group filters, search, leader-key shortcuts (G prefix) and `?` overlay, ESLint config and CI grep checks (innerHTML, eval, new Function, emoji, em-dash).
- Step 6 complete: service worker (sw.js) with cache-first shell and data-shard cache, build-hash-keyed cache name, navigation fallback to index.html when offline. App registers SW only on https or localhost.
- Step 7 complete: scripts/build-data.mjs produces 24 shards across 9 datasets (physical-constants, electrical, plumbing, hvac, restoration, construction, fire, crosswalks, summaries) with per-folder manifest.json and SHA-256 hashes; scripts/verify-integrity.mjs checks every shard against scripts/expected-hashes.json; scripts/sources.md records provenance.
- Step 8 complete: pure-math.js library implementing AWG geometry, conductor resistance at temperature, ampacity from heat balance, voltage drop, single- and three-phase power, Hazen-Williams, Darcy-Weisbach with Colebrook iteration, beam mechanics, allowable spans by bending and deflection, psychrometrics (August-Roche-Magnus), refrigerant P-T linear interpolation, fire hose friction (CQ^2L), hydrant flow, temperature conversions. 41 unit tests passing on the Node built-in runner.
- Step 9 complete: Group A Electrical (utilities 1 through 11) in calc-electrical.js. Live-rendered calculator views with Test-with-example buttons, Copy affordances, inline citations, and aria-live output regions for Ohm's Law, Wire Ampacity, Voltage Drop, Conduit Fill, Box Fill, Breaker Sizing, Motor FLA, Transformer Sizing, Three-Phase Power, Conductor Resistance at Temperature, EGC Sizing. Renderers wired into app.js. 23 additional unit tests, 75 total passing.
- Step 10 complete: Group B Plumbing and Gas (utilities 12 through 20) in calc-plumbing.js. Hunter's-Curve fixture-unit pipe sizing, Hazen-Williams and Darcy-Weisbach friction loss, pipe volume, hydraulic-hp pump sizing, static pressure with elevation, Spitzglass gas pipe sizing, slope, NIST SP 811-based pressure conversion, backflow reference. 23 additional unit tests, 98 total passing.
- Step 11 complete: Group C HVAC (utilities 21 through 31) in calc-hvac.js. Simplified Manual J cooling and heating estimators, Darcy-Weisbach duct sizing with Colebrook iteration, static pressure summation, refrigerant P-T chart for R-410A/R-32/R-22/R-134a/R-404A/R-407C with manufacturer attribution, superheat and subcool, SEER/EER conversion, heat-pump balance point, SHR, CFM per ton, combustion air. Manual J cooling and heating and duct sizing run in manual-j-worker.js Web Worker (with in-thread fallback for tests). 27 additional unit tests, 125 total passing.
- Step 12 complete: Group D Restoration (utilities 32 through 39) in calc-restoration.js. Psychrometric calculator (dew point, GPP, vapor pressure), drying goal (target GPP and indoor RH), AHAM and field-method dehumidifier sizing, air mover placement by water class, IICRC water classes/categories reference, material drying times reference, mold growth risk, PPE selection by water category. 19 additional unit tests, 144 total passing.
- Step 13 complete: Group E Carpentry and Construction (utilities 40 through 50) in calc-construction.js. Stair geometry, roof pitch, rafter length, square footage (rectangle/triangle/trapezoid/circle), board footage, concrete volume (slab/footing/column/footing-with-stem), rebar quantity, lumber spans (first-principles beam mechanics with bundled species/grade properties), nail/screw withdrawal capacity (G^2.5 * D * 1380), beam loading (uniform and centered point), material quantity for common assemblies. 28 additional unit tests, 172 total passing.
- Step 14 complete: Group F Fire-Ground Engineering (utilities 51 through 58) in calc-fire.js. CQ^2L hose friction with NFA coefficients (1.5/1.75/2.5/3/4/5 in), pump discharge pressure (with 0.5 psi/ft elevation), hydrant flow, ISO needed-fire-flow estimator, master-stream reach, aerial-ladder reach, foam concentrate volume, smoke reading reference. 17 additional unit tests, 189 total passing.
- Step 15 complete: Group G Cross-Trade (utilities 59 through 64) in calc-cross.js. Comprehensive unit converter (length, area, volume, mass, force, pressure, energy, power, flow, electrical voltage/current/resistance/capacitance, temperature with affine handling), material cost estimator with optional tax and delivery, markup/margin calculator (bidirectional), time and materials estimator with overhead and profit, sales tax with bundled state rates and override, tip-out splitter. 24 additional unit tests, 213 total passing.
- Step 16 complete: Lighthouse CI configured at lighthouserc.json with FCP < 1s, LCP < 1.5s, TBT < 100ms, CLS < 0.05, score >= 95 across performance/accessibility/best-practices/SEO; runs in .github/workflows/ci.yml against home view plus three representative utility views. docs/performance.md documents the budget. .github/workflows/data-refresh.yml schedules the monthly data pipeline and opens a PR if shards change.
- Step 17 complete: Playwright + axe-core integration tests at test/integration/a11y.test.js covering WCAG 2.2 AA across 16 representative views, single-h1 invariant, focused h1 on tool views, aria-pressed toggling on filter buttons, and 48x48 minimum touch targets. test/integration/playwright.config.js spawns a same-origin static server. CI-only dev dependency; npm run test:e2e and test:a11y wired to Playwright. index.html title and theme-color meta added.
- Step 18 complete: _headers file at the repository root carries CSP (default/script/style/img/connect/form-action/base-uri 'self', frame-ancestors 'none', object-src 'none', worker-src 'self'), HSTS one-year preload, X-Content-Type-Options nosniff, X-Frame-Options DENY, Referrer-Policy no-referrer, COOP same-origin, COEP require-corp, CORP same-origin, Permissions-Policy disabling camera/microphone/geolocation/payment/USB/accelerometer/gyroscope/magnetometer. CSP meta tag in index.html updated to match. robots.txt, sitemap.xml, and site.webmanifest added.
- Step 19 complete: First-principles verification suite at test/unit/first-principles.test.js cross-checks copper resistance per kft (within 5% of published DC values), ampacity at 75 C / 30 C ambient (within 30% of NEC 75 C column), Hazen-Williams worked example, refrigerant P-T at bundled table points, lumber spans (within 20% of published-equivalent values for representative joists), NFA hose friction, and hydrant flow. CI workflow at .github/workflows/ci.yml runs lint, unit, data:verify, Lighthouse, and accessibility on every push and PR; data-refresh workflow runs monthly. 220 unit tests passing.
- Step 20 complete: scripts/analyze-data-changes.mjs walks each per-folder manifest, diffs current shards against the previous git revision, and emits a Markdown summary covering changed/added/removed shards with old/new hashes plus per-shard added/modified/removed entries (with drill-down into values/rates/refrigerants/summaries layers). Wired into the data-refresh workflow as the PR body. Footer Changelog link added to index.html.
- Step 21 complete: scripts/build.mjs copies the static shell, all calculator modules, _headers, robots.txt, sitemap.xml, site.webmanifest, CHANGELOG, LICENSE, and the data/ tree into dist/, plus a build-info.json with the build timestamp. scripts/dev.mjs is a Node-only static server with the production CSP applied for local development. npm run dev / build / clean wired. docs/deployment.md documents the Cloudflare Pages configuration. Build output: 53 files, ~290 KB.
- Step 22 complete: docs/launch-checklist.md is the written report per spec section 14 step 22. 19 items pass locally with automated assertions; 11 items are gated on first-deploy verification (Mozilla Observatory A+, securityheaders.com A+, HSTS preload submission, CSP enforcement in console, deployed offline behavior, deployed Lighthouse run). 220 unit tests passing, lint clean, data-integrity passing.
